					<description><![CDATA[<p>A list of Udemy's 250 most popular online courses. Combined, they've gathered 79.5 million enrollments.</p>
<p>The post <a rel="nofollow" href="https://www.classcentral.com/report/udemy-top-courses/">[2023] 250 Top Udemy Courses of All Time</a> appeared first on <a rel="nofollow" href="https://www.classcentral.com/report">The Report by Class Central</a>.</p>
]]></description>
										<content:encoded><![CDATA[<p><a href="https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2021/01/udemy-top-courses.png"><img loading="lazy" class="alignnone size-full wp-image-73861" src="https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2021/01/udemy-top-courses.png" alt="Udemy Top Courses" width="1024" height="512" srcset="https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2021/01/udemy-top-courses.png 1024w, https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2021/01/udemy-top-courses-300x150.png 300w, https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2021/01/udemy-top-courses-768x384.png 768w" sizes="(max-width: 1024px) 100vw, 1024px" /></a></p>
<p><a href="https://www.classcentral.com/provider/udemy">Udemy</a> is one of the largest online learning platforms for professional learning. <a href="https://about.udemy.com/">According to the company</a>, they have 57 million registered users. An <a href="https://www.classcentral.com/report/udemy-by-the-numbers/">analysis by Class Central</a> shows they’ve launched over 200,000 courses since 2010.</p>
<p>The pandemic boosted the <a href="https://www.classcentral.com/report/mooc-stats-pandemic/">fortune of many online providers</a>. Udemy was no exception. In 2020, <a href="https://www.classcentral.com/report/the-second-year-of-the-mooc/">propelled by the pandemic</a>, they <a href="https://www.crunchbase.com/organization/udemy/company_financials">raised $123 million</a> and increased their valuation by over $1 billion.</p>
<p>In 2022, the situation changed. Overall, the company raised ~$300 million at a valuation over <a href="https://www.businesswire.com/news/home/20201118005326/en/Udemy-Raises-50-Million-to-Fuel-Accelerated-Global-Demand-for-Online-Learning">$3 billion</a>. But Udemy&#8217;s market cap has significantly <a href="https://www.classcentral.com/report/2022-year-in-review/">fallen, like that of many other online course platforms</a>.</p>
<p>In this course ranking, let&#8217;s explore the best of the best that Udemy has to offer.</p>
<h2>Udemy By the Numbers</h2>
<figure id="attachment_84875" aria-describedby="caption-attachment-84875" style="width: 1536px" class="wp-caption alignnone"><a href="https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2021/01/Growth-of-Courses_1.png"><img loading="lazy" class="size-full wp-image-84875" src="https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2021/01/Growth-of-Courses_1.png" alt="" width="1536" height="768" srcset="https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2021/01/Growth-of-Courses_1.png 1536w, https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2021/01/Growth-of-Courses_1-300x150.png 300w, https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2021/01/Growth-of-Courses_1-1024x512.png 1024w, https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2021/01/Growth-of-Courses_1-768x384.png 768w" sizes="(max-width: 1536px) 100vw, 1536px" /></a><figcaption id="caption-attachment-84875" class="wp-caption-text">Udemy By the Numbers (Jan 2023)</figcaption></figure>
<p>Analyzing Udemy&#8217;s catalog with my colleague <a href="https://www.classcentral.com/@archisha">@Archisha</a>, we discovered that they currently have over 202,000 courses — which amounts to a 33% increase in the last 2 years. You may find a complete analysis of Udemy&#8217;s catalog here: <a href="https://www.classcentral.com/report/udemy-by-the-numbers/">202K Courses, 662M Enrollments: Breaking Down Udemy’s Massive Catalog</a>.</p>
<p>Combined, Udemy’s 202K courses have gathered ~662 million enrollments and average 3274 enrollments per course. What I found most surprising is that the median enrollment is only 240, which means that half of Udemy’s courses don’t reach 240 learners.</p>
<p>Currently, there are 718 courses with over 100K enrollments and 4 courses with over a million enrollments.</p>
<p>Do Udemy courses satisfy the <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Pareto_principle">Pareto 80/20 principle</a>? I found that Udemy’s top-20% courses by enrollment account for 91% of all enrollments.</p>
<p>You can also find some of the <a href="https://www.classcentral.com/provider/udemy">best Udemy courses</a> on Class Central&#8217;s catalog page.</p>
<hr />
<h2>250 Top Udemy Courses</h2>
<p>Here&#8217;s a quick summary of 250 Udemy top courses based on the number of enrollments:</p>
<ul>
<li>Enrollments range from <strong>187K</strong> to <strong>1.8M</strong>. There are 4 courses with over <strong>1M</strong> enrollments.</li>
<li>Combined, they account for <strong>79.5M</strong> enrollments, with an average of <strong>318K</strong> enrollments.</li>
<li><strong>31%</strong> of the courses are free.</li>
<li><strong>90%</strong> of the courses are in English.</li>
<li aria-level="1">Combined, they represent <strong>4K</strong> hours of content.</li>
</ul>

										<content:encoded><![CDATA[<figure id="attachment_85288" aria-describedby="caption-attachment-85288" style="width: 1024px" class="wp-caption alignnone"><img loading="lazy" class="size-full wp-image-85288" src="https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2023/02/Goldman-Sachs-10000-Women-Jiyoung-Host.png" alt="" width="1024" height="512" srcset="https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2023/02/Goldman-Sachs-10000-Women-Jiyoung-Host.png 1024w, https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2023/02/Goldman-Sachs-10000-Women-Jiyoung-Host-300x150.png 300w, https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2023/02/Goldman-Sachs-10000-Women-Jiyoung-Host-768x384.png 768w" sizes="(max-width: 1024px) 100vw, 1024px" /><figcaption id="caption-attachment-85288" class="wp-caption-text">Jiyoung, host.</figcaption></figure>
<h2>Introduction</h2>
<p><a href="https://www.classcentral.com/institution/goldmansachs">Goldman Sachs</a> has released a series of 10 short courses in their 10,000 Women series. They are also available in Spanish, Portuguese, and Hindi. I have taken three courses so far and here are my reviews.</p>
<h2><a href="https://www.classcentral.com/course/10k-women-2-19373">Fundamentals of Business Finance</a></h2>
<figure id="attachment_85289" aria-describedby="caption-attachment-85289" style="width: 1024px" class="wp-caption alignnone"><img loading="lazy" class="size-full wp-image-85289" src="https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2023/02/Fundamentals-of-Business-Finance-with-Goldman-Sachs-10000-Women-What-is-an-Income-Statement_.png" alt="" width="1024" height="512" srcset="https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2023/02/Fundamentals-of-Business-Finance-with-Goldman-Sachs-10000-Women-What-is-an-Income-Statement_.png 1024w, https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2023/02/Fundamentals-of-Business-Finance-with-Goldman-Sachs-10000-Women-What-is-an-Income-Statement_-300x150.png 300w, https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2023/02/Fundamentals-of-Business-Finance-with-Goldman-Sachs-10000-Women-What-is-an-Income-Statement_-768x384.png 768w" sizes="(max-width: 1024px) 100vw, 1024px" /><figcaption id="caption-attachment-85289" class="wp-caption-text">From &#8220;What is an Income Statement&#8221; lesson.</figcaption></figure>
<p>This course really opened my eyes to see all my previous losses, what I did wrong and how to improve in my business. The confidence of accountability I have now in my business is a result of this course.</p>
<h2><a href="https://www.classcentral.com/course/10k-women-3-19369">Fundamentals of Leadership</a></h2>
<figure id="attachment_85290" aria-describedby="caption-attachment-85290" style="width: 1024px" class="wp-caption alignnone"><img loading="lazy" class="size-full wp-image-85290" src="https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2023/02/Fundamentals-of-Leadership-with-Goldman-Sachs-10000-Women.png" alt="" width="1024" height="512" srcset="https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2023/02/Fundamentals-of-Leadership-with-Goldman-Sachs-10000-Women.png 1024w, https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2023/02/Fundamentals-of-Leadership-with-Goldman-Sachs-10000-Women-300x150.png 300w, https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2023/02/Fundamentals-of-Leadership-with-Goldman-Sachs-10000-Women-768x384.png 768w" sizes="(max-width: 1024px) 100vw, 1024px" /><figcaption id="caption-attachment-85290" class="wp-caption-text">What is your leadership style?</figcaption></figure>
<p>This course made me identify my mission and vision statement, also knowing my core values for my business.</p>
<p>This course really made me read and understand what I actually want in a business, how I want my environment to be, and how I intend to make my staff feel while working for me. This course is everything any business owner needs to go through.</p>
<p>With this course, you will have the need to get to actually know your staff: how to place them and rate their performance as they work for you; Giving them room to discuss and showcase their talents and their opinions really matters in a business. I always have this slogan I use when advising business owners: “The way you treat your staff will determine the rate at which they will help to grow your business. 75% of staff will always want positive results for their employer’s business while 25% will just want to work and earn a salary not minding how the business succeeds.” Treating your staff right can help save your business in the sense that nobody wants to lose the job they value and get treated right.</p>
<div class="quote relative padding-horz-large xlarge-up-padding-horz-xxlarge padding-vert-xxsmall margin-bottom-large quote-pull quote-text">
<p>Attention to details: staff tends to pay great attention to details and their environment when the workplace is accommodating.<span class="quote_deco absolute top left height-100"> </span></p>
</div>
<p>To conclude, every business owner needs to embark on self discovery to find their purpose and they should also work on their expectations.</p>
<h2><a href="https://www.classcentral.com/course/gs10kw-11222">Grow Your Business</a></h2>
<figure id="attachment_85291" aria-describedby="caption-attachment-85291" style="width: 1024px" class="wp-caption alignnone"><img loading="lazy" class="size-full wp-image-85291" src="https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2023/02/Grow-Your-Business-with-Goldman-Sachs-10000-Women-Selecting-a-growth-opportunity-Kalyani-Study-Case.png" alt="" width="1024" height="512" srcset="https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2023/02/Grow-Your-Business-with-Goldman-Sachs-10000-Women-Selecting-a-growth-opportunity-Kalyani-Study-Case.png 1024w, https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2023/02/Grow-Your-Business-with-Goldman-Sachs-10000-Women-Selecting-a-growth-opportunity-Kalyani-Study-Case-300x150.png 300w, https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2023/02/Grow-Your-Business-with-Goldman-Sachs-10000-Women-Selecting-a-growth-opportunity-Kalyani-Study-Case-768x384.png 768w" sizes="(max-width: 1024px) 100vw, 1024px" /><figcaption id="caption-attachment-85291" class="wp-caption-text">From &#8220;Selecting a growth opportunity&#8221; lesson, Ancient Living study case.</figcaption></figure>
<p>This course will make you see the need for growth in your business and work towards it. You will source for funds to expand your business in all areas.</p>
<p>I came across this course and decided to go for it because the little business I run doesn’t get a good turnover so I needed to generate more ideas for growth. Having an opportunity in the business helps maximize your growth potential. With this course, you will be able to select a growth opportunity alongside preparing you to generate ideas for more growth opportunities.</p>
<h2>What’s next</h2>
<p>I plan to take more courses in the <a href="https://www.classcentral.com/institution/goldmansachs">Goldman Sachs 10,000 Women</a> series.</p>

<h2><span style="font-weight: 400;">What is Japanese (Language)?</span></h2>
<p><span style="font-weight: 400;">Japanese (日本語, Nihongo) is the native language primarily spoken by the people of Japan where it is the national language. Japanese belongs to the </span><a target="_blank" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Japonic_languages" rel="noopener"><span style="font-weight: 400;">Japonic</span></a><span style="font-weight: 400;"> or Japanese-Ryukyuan language family.</span></p>
<h3><span style="font-weight: 400;">Hiragana, Katakana, and Kanji</span></h3>
<p><span style="font-weight: 400;">The Japanese language uses three scripts: Hiragana, Katakana, and Kanji. Let’s take a quick look at each of them.</span></p>
<figure id="attachment_85263" aria-describedby="caption-attachment-85263" style="width: 1537px" class="wp-caption alignnone"><img loading="lazy" class="size-full wp-image-85263" src="https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2023/02/The-three-scripts.png" alt="" width="1537" height="769" srcset="https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2023/02/The-three-scripts.png 1537w, https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2023/02/The-three-scripts-300x150.png 300w, https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2023/02/The-three-scripts-1024x512.png 1024w, https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2023/02/The-three-scripts-768x384.png 768w" sizes="(max-width: 1537px) 100vw, 1537px" /><figcaption id="caption-attachment-85263" class="wp-caption-text">The three scripts (<a target="_blank" href="https://www.classcentral.com/course/udemy-learn-japanese-for-beginners-26156" rel="noopener">Learn Japanese for Beginners: The Ultimate 100-Lesson Course</a>)</figcaption></figure>
<p><b>Hiragana</b><span style="font-weight: 400;"> is used to write functional words and particles. Hiragana is like the basic Japanese alphabet and consists of 46 characters.</span></p>
<p><b>Katakana</b><span style="font-weight: 400;"> is used to write foreign words and names. Katakana is almost exactly the same as Hiragana with 46 characters except that it is written slightly differently.</span></p>
<p><b>Kanji</b><span style="font-weight: 400;"> is used to write native Japanese words or words of Chinese origin. Kanji characters represent an idea or concept and act more like entire words than individual letters. There are over 2,000 Kanji characters!</span></p>
<h3><span style="font-weight: 400;">Japanese Proficiency Test: JLPT</span></h3>
<p><span style="font-weight: 400;">The </span><a target="_blank" href="https://www.jlpt.jp/e/index.html" rel="noopener"><span style="font-weight: 400;">Japanese-Language Proficiency Test</span></a><span style="font-weight: 400;"> (JLPT), offered by the Japan Foundation and Japan Educational Exchanges and Services, is the largest-scale Japanese-language test in the world. It is held worldwide to evaluate and certify proficiency in Japanese of non-native speakers. Language proficiency is tested on the basis of reading and listening, as well as vocabulary and grammar.</span></p>
<p><span style="font-weight: 400;">The JLPT has five levels, N1, N2, N3, N4 and N5, the level of difficulty increasing from N5 to N1. Below is a summary of the linguistic competence required for each level as described by </span><a target="_blank" href="https://www.jlpt.jp/e/about/levelsummary.html" rel="noopener"><span style="font-weight: 400;">JLPT</span></a><span style="font-weight: 400;">.</span></p>
<table>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td><b>N1</b></td>
<td><span style="font-weight: 400;">The ability to understand Japanese used in a variety of circumstances.</span></td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td><b>N2</b></td>
<td><span style="font-weight: 400;">The ability to understand Japanese used in everyday situations, and in a variety of circumstances to a certain degree.</span></td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td><b>N3</b></td>
<td><span style="font-weight: 400;">The ability to understand Japanese used in everyday situations to a certain degree.</span></td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td><b>N4</b></td>
<td><span style="font-weight: 400;">The ability to understand basic Japanese.</span></td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td><b>N5</b></td>
<td><span style="font-weight: 400;">The ability to understand some basic Japanese.</span></td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>
<h3><span style="font-weight: 400;">Why are Japanese Skills Important?</span></h3>
<p><span style="font-weight: 400;">Among the </span><a target="_blank" href="https://joyofjapanese.com/why-learn-japanese/" rel="noopener"><span style="font-weight: 400;">many reasons to learn Japanese</span></a><span style="font-weight: 400;"> there are a few that stand out: Being able to communicate with over 125 million native speakers (Japanese is the 8th </span><a target="_blank" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/List_of_languages_by_number_of_native_speakers" rel="noopener"><span style="font-weight: 400;">most spoken language in the world</span></a><span style="font-weight: 400;">), enjoying one of the most popular cultures in the world with its unique cuisine, music and movie industry, and most importantly, animes in their original language. These are more than enough reasons to convince any language aficionado to get started learning Japanese. </span></p>
<p><span style="font-weight: 400;">In addition to that, Japan is also known for its tech and automobile industry, bringing to the world a number of </span><a target="_blank" href="https://blog.japanwondertravel.com/largest-and-popular-japanese-companies-34000" rel="noopener"><span style="font-weight: 400;">large Japanese companies</span></a><span style="font-weight: 400;"> (such as Nintendo, Toyota, Canon, Sony, etc.) that carry in their core a strong culture attached to Japan roots.</span></p>
<p><span style="font-weight: 400;">And lastly, if you want to open up to a number of opportunities as a Japanese translator or interpreter to your own language, there are hundreds of job openings on </span><a target="_blank" href="https://www.indeed.com/q-Japanese-Translator-jobs.html?vjk=6566af5e8b50f060" rel="noopener"><span style="font-weight: 400;">Indeed</span></a><span style="font-weight: 400;">, </span><a target="_blank" href="https://www.upwork.com/freelance-jobs/translation-japanese-english/" rel="noopener"><span style="font-weight: 400;">Upwork</span></a><span style="font-weight: 400;"> and </span><a target="_blank" href="https://www.linkedin.com/jobs/japanese-translator-jobs/?currentJobId=3307031894" rel="noopener"><span style="font-weight: 400;">LinkedIn</span></a><span style="font-weight: 400;">. You can also work as a language instructor or even diversify your reach as a tour guide and help Japanese travelers visiting your country.</span></p>
<h3><span style="font-weight: 400;">What is My Experience with Japanese?</span></h3>
<p><span style="font-weight: 400;">I’ve learned a bit of Japanese mainly from anime, J-pop and Japanese movies. As my interest grew, I started learning more about Japan in general, so I became familiar with how Japanese actually works in the real world. Hearing real people talk gave me more enthusiasm to learn the language and explore the country as well.</span></p>
<p><span style="font-weight: 400;">Besides that, I am a </span><a target="_blank" href="https://www.coursera.org/instructor/archisha-bhar" rel="noopener"><span style="font-weight: 400;">Guided Project Instructor</span></a><span style="font-weight: 400;"> and a Beta Tester at Coursera, having tested many courses before they’re officially launched. I have taken </span><a target="_blank" href="https://www.classcentral.com/@archisha" rel="noopener"><span style="font-weight: 400;">over 50 online courses</span></a><span style="font-weight: 400;"> in various subjects.</span></p>
<p><span style="font-weight: 400;">My experience as an online learner and teacher has given me some perspective on what to look for in an online course. I used my experience to evaluate each course in this list.</span></p>
<p><a target="_blank" href="https://www.classcentral.com" rel="noopener"><img loading="lazy" class="alignnone wp-image-79248 size-full" src="https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2022/03/Class-Central-Preview-2.png" alt="Find your next course on Class Central" width="1024" height="512" srcset="https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2022/03/Class-Central-Preview-2.png 1024w, https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2022/03/Class-Central-Preview-2-300x150.png 300w, https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2022/03/Class-Central-Preview-2-768x384.png 768w" sizes="(max-width: 1024px) 100vw, 1024px" /></a></p>
<h2><span style="font-weight: 400;">Course Ranking Methodology</span></h2>
<p><span style="font-weight: 400;">I built this ranking following the now tried-and-tested methodology I used in previous rankings (</span><a target="_blank" href="https://www.classcentral.com/report/category/best-courses/" rel="noopener"><span style="font-weight: 400;">you can find them all here</span></a><span style="font-weight: 400;">). It involves a three-step process:</span></p>
<ol>
<li style="font-weight: 400;" aria-level="1"><b>Research:</b><span style="font-weight: 400;"> I started by leveraging Class Central’s database with </span><a target="_blank" href="https://www.classcentral.com/subjects" rel="noopener"><span style="font-weight: 400;">100K online courses</span></a><span style="font-weight: 400;"> and 200K+ reviews. Then, I made a preliminary selection of </span><a target="_blank" href="https://www.classcentral.com/subject/japanese" rel="noopener"><span style="font-weight: 400;">40+ Japanese courses</span></a><span style="font-weight: 400;"> by rating, reviews, and bookmarks.</span></li>
<li style="font-weight: 400;" aria-level="1"><b>Evaluate:</b><span style="font-weight: 400;"> I read through reviews on Class Central, Reddit, and course providers to understand what other learners thought about each course and combined it with my own experience as a </span><a target="_blank" href="https://www.classcentral.com/@archisha" rel="noopener"><span style="font-weight: 400;">learner</span></a><span style="font-weight: 400;">.</span></li>
<li style="font-weight: 400;" aria-level="1"><b>Select:</b><span style="font-weight: 400;"> Well-made courses were picked if they presented valuable and engaging content and they have to fit in a set of criteria and be ranked accordingly: comprehensive curriculum, release date, affordability, ratings and enrollments.</span></li>
</ol>
<p><span style="font-weight: 400;">The end result is a unique selection of courses that combines a decade of Class Central data and my own experience as an online learner to try to get the best of both worlds. So far, I’ve spent more than 10 hours building this list, and I’ll continue to update it.</span></p>
<h2><span style="font-weight: 400;">Course Ranking Statistics</span></h2>
<p><span style="font-weight: 400;">Here are some statistics regarding this course ranking:</span></p>
<ul>
<li style="font-weight: 400;" aria-level="1"><span style="font-weight: 400;">Combined, these courses have accrued over </span><b>197K</b><span style="font-weight: 400;"> enrollments.</span></li>
<li style="font-weight: 400;" aria-level="1"><span style="font-weight: 400;">5 courses are </span><b>free</b><span style="font-weight: 400;"> or </span><b>free-to-audit</b><span style="font-weight: 400;"> and 5 courses are </span><b>paid</b><span style="font-weight: 400;">.</span></li>
<li style="font-weight: 400;" aria-level="1"><span style="font-weight: 400;">The most-represented course provider in the ranking is </span><b>Udemy</b><span style="font-weight: 400;">, with 5 courses.</span></li>
<li style="font-weight: 400;" aria-level="1"><span style="font-weight: 400;">8 courses are in English and 2 courses are in Japanese (subtitles available).</span></li>

<h3><span style="font-weight: 400;">Fun Facts</span></h3>
<ul>
<li style="font-weight: 400;" aria-level="1"><span style="font-weight: 400;">According to the </span><a target="_blank" href="https://japansociety.org/about/" rel="noopener"><span style="font-weight: 400;">JapanSociety.org</span></a><span style="font-weight: 400;">, “Japan Society was founded on May 19, 1907 by a group of prominent New York business people and philanthropists, many of whom shaped the policies of exchange and collaboration that guided the Society until the outbreak of World War II. After the war, activities slowly resumed, and the stewardship of John D. Rockefeller 3rd from 1952 to 1978 led to a unified vision, a firm financial foundation, and a revitalized mission that continues to inspire and sustain the organization today.”</span></li>
<li style="font-weight: 400;" aria-level="1"><span style="font-weight: 400;">Founded in 1972, </span><a target="_blank" href="https://japansociety.org/language-center/" rel="noopener"><span style="font-weight: 400;">Japan Society’s Language Center</span></a><span style="font-weight: 400;"> is the premiere venue for learning Japanese in New York City.</span></li>
</ul>

					<description><![CDATA[<p>Here is a guide with the best online courses (including free ones) to learn Erlang, a programming language designed for building scalable, fault-tolerant systems.</p>
<p>The post <a rel="nofollow" href="https://www.classcentral.com/report/best-erlang-courses/">7 Best Erlang Courses to Take in 2023</a> appeared first on <a rel="nofollow" href="https://www.classcentral.com/report">The Report by Class Central</a>.</p>

										<content:encoded><![CDATA[<p><img loading="lazy" class="alignnone size-full wp-image-85268" src="https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2023/02/Erlang-BCG-Banner.png" alt="" width="1024" height="512" srcset="https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2023/02/Erlang-BCG-Banner.png 1024w, https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2023/02/Erlang-BCG-Banner-300x150.png 300w, https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2023/02/Erlang-BCG-Banner-768x384.png 768w" sizes="(max-width: 1024px) 100vw, 1024px" /></p>
<p>WhatsApp. Cisco. GoDaddy. IBM. Heroku. What do they all have in common?</p>
<p>They all use Erlang in their technology stack!</p>
<p>Erlang is a programming language specifically designed for building scalable, fault-tolerant systems that can run smoothly in a distributed environment. Its unique approach to concurrency and message-passing makes it ideal for building real-time, high-traffic systems like WhatsApp&#8217;s messaging platform, Cisco&#8217;s networking equipment, GoDaddy&#8217;s hosting services, IBM&#8217;s cloud offerings, and Heroku&#8217;s platform as a service. In fact, <a href="https://erlang-companies.org/companies/cisco.html" target="_blank" rel="noopener">90% of all internet traffic goes through Erlang controlled nodes</a>.</p>
<p>Want to find out and learn more about this (kind of) unknown yet powerful language? Continue reading to see my picks for the best Erlang courses. Click on one to skip to the course details:</p>

<tbody>

<td>Best <b>free</b> course for beginner Erlang programmers to master practical Erlang</td>

<h2>What is Erlang?</h2>
<p>Erlang is a general-purpose functional programming language and runtime environment developed by Ericsson, a Swedish telecommunications company, in the 1980s. The team needed a programming language that can handle <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Telephone_exchange" target="_blank" rel="noopener">telephone switching</a> — a very difficult endeavor that requires high levels of concurrency and zero downtime (I’m sure you can imagine why).</p>
<p>After experimenting with dozens of different languages, they came to a stark conclusion: no such language exists! Instead of giving up or settling for compromises, they instead decided to create their own programming language.</p>
<p>Hopefully that brief history lesson gave you some context for why Erlang is known for two things: its practical concurrent programming and its robust virtual machine.</p>
<p>Erlang is a functional programming language for all the right reasons — scalability and concurrency. It has a <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Actor_model" target="_blank" rel="noopener">lightweight threading model</a> (which Rust also uses) and a powerful process-based runtime system. <a href="https://erlang.org/course/history.html" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Companies like WhatsApp and Heroku</a> are able to scale and handle millions of concurrent connections in real-time thanks to Erlang.</p>
<p>Also, the Erlang virtual machine (BEAM) is legendary for its fault-tolerance. The language has built-in support for handling failures, like automatically restarting processes and recovering from crashes. For mission-critical systems, you can be rest assured that your applications will continue running 24/7 even when things eventually go wrong.</p>
<p>In addition to its concurrency and fault tolerance features, Erlang is also a highly expressive language that allows you to write concise and elegant code. It has a simple syntax and a rich set of libraries, like the Open Telecom Platform, making it easy to learn and use.</p>
<p>Unfortunately, there are not enough developers in the world that know Erlang, even though Erlang developers are highly sought after. That’s why Erlang is the second highest paying programming language to learn (after Clojure) according to the <a href="https://survey.stackoverflow.co/2022/" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Stack Overflow Developer Survey 2022</a>. So why not become one of them? Whether you&#8217;re building a web application, a real-time messaging system, or a distributed database, Erlang is a worthy choice for building reliable, scalable systems.</p>

<h2 id="anchor-1">1. <a href="https://www.classcentral.com/course/youtube-erlang-tutorial-120161" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Erlang Tutorial (Erlang Tutorial)</a></h2>
<p><img loading="lazy" class="alignnone size-full wp-image-85269" src="https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2023/02/1.-Erlang-Tutorial-Erlang-Tutorial.png" alt="" width="1024" height="512" srcset="https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2023/02/1.-Erlang-Tutorial-Erlang-Tutorial.png 1024w, https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2023/02/1.-Erlang-Tutorial-Erlang-Tutorial-300x150.png 300w, https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2023/02/1.-Erlang-Tutorial-Erlang-Tutorial-768x384.png 768w" sizes="(max-width: 1024px) 100vw, 1024px" /></p>
<p>My #1 pick for the best course to learn Erlang is the <a href="https://www.classcentral.com/course/youtube-erlang-tutorial-120161" target="_blank" rel="noopener"><i>Erlang Tutorial</i></a> playlist.</p>
<p>I chose this course as my top pick because it is both recent and comprehensive. Plus, the video tutorials teach Erlang through interactive programming and examples. By the end of this tutorial, you’ll have a well-grounded understanding of the Erlang programming language.</p>
<p>Some prior knowledge of programming is required to take this course.</p>
<h3>What You’ll Learn</h3>
<p>In this tutorial, you’ll start by learning the tools and vocabulary of the Erlang programming language. You’ll write a simple &#8220;Hello, World&#8221; module and compile it to get a feel for the Erlang syntax and structure. You’ll then delve into common programming concepts such as data types, control structures, and functions, but with a functional and concurrent twist specific to Erlang.</p>
<p>One of the key features of Erlang is its use of processes to execute code concurrently (fun fact, millions of processes can run at the same time!). You’ll learn how to spawn and manage them. Other functional programming concepts will be explored too, such as recursion, anonymous functions, and higher-order functions. Along with other concepts like atoms, comprehensions, and pattern matching, you’ll have the skills to write efficient and scalable code.</p>
<p>In addition to these foundational topics, you’ll study more advanced constructs in Erlang. You’ll learn how to use maps and processes together to build a simple key-value database that can perform basic data operations. You’ll also learn about error handling in Erlang, and how to design your code to continue running even when errors occur. And to give you some practical examples, you’ll implement a palindrome checker and Conway&#8217;s game of life in Erlang, giving you the opportunity to apply your knowledge to real-world problems.</p>
<h3>How You’ll Learn</h3>
<p>This course is 8–9 hours long. You’ll learn by watching the lecture videos and following along with the instructor as he codes interactively using the Erlang shell.</p>

<h2 id="anchor-2">2. <a href="https://www.classcentral.com/course/independent-erlang-master-classes-120166" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Erlang Master Classes (University of Kent)</a></h2>
<p><img loading="lazy" class="alignnone size-full wp-image-85270" src="https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2023/02/2.-Erlang-Master-Classes-University-of-Kent.png" alt="" width="1024" height="512" srcset="https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2023/02/2.-Erlang-Master-Classes-University-of-Kent.png 1024w, https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2023/02/2.-Erlang-Master-Classes-University-of-Kent-300x150.png 300w, https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2023/02/2.-Erlang-Master-Classes-University-of-Kent-768x384.png 768w" sizes="(max-width: 1024px) 100vw, 1024px" /></p>
<p>My 2nd pick for the best Erlang course are <a href="https://www.classcentral.com/course/independent-erlang-master-classes-120166" target="_blank" rel="noopener">the Erlang Master Classes</a> from the University of Kent.</p>
<p>This <b>free</b> course comprises three master classes taught by esteemed Erlang programmers (one of them even helped invent Erlang). Each class focuses on different aspects of Erlang — functional programming, concurrent programming, and larger-scale programming with OTP — are used to solve complex real-world problems through case studies and examples. By the end of the course, you’ll know how Erlang is used practically.</p>
<p>The course assumes you have some basic familiarity with Erlang (watch the first video of the first masterclass to know more).</p>
<h3>What You’ll Learn</h3>
<p>The first master class focuses on language processing in general, with a focus on processing arithmetical expressions in Erlang. This will include how to interpret, compile, and run the expressions on a virtual machine, as well as simplifying and converting them to and from a textual form.</p>
<p>In the second master class, you’ll understand how Erlang does concurrent programming in Erlang through the ‘share nothing’ concurrency model. You’ll learn how to make sequential code concurrent and how to build systems using communicating processes. You’ll also cover Erlang’s famous approach to fault tolerance and how errors can happen while still keeping the program running.</p>
<p>Erlang has a wide ecosystem of tools and libraries — that’s what makes Erlang great. But, the most important tool for servers is arguably the The Open Telecom Platform (OTP). Hence in the final master class, you’ll explore OTP in depth, taking a look at its generic behaviors (such as a generic server) and how it can be used to build complex systems quickly and reliably, in addition to packaging and releasing systems.</p>
<h3>How You’ll Learn</h3>
<p>The master classes are presented by Joe Armstrong, Ericsson AB and KTH, Stockholm, and one of the inventors of Erlang; Francesco Cesarini, CTO and founder of Erlang Solutions Ltd; and Simon Thompson, functional programming teacher and researcher at the University of Kent. Each Master Class ends with a discussion between the three presenters on some of the issues raised by the Master Class.</p>

<li aria-level="1">Joe Armstrong is one of the “gang of three” Erlang inventors, and a champion of the Erlang approach to programming large complex systems. He has worked for Ericsson, as well as in startups, and is also professor at KTH, Stockholm.</li>
<li aria-level="1">Francesco Cesarini is the founder and Technical Director of Erlang Solutions Ltd, the company focused on building scalable, reliable systems based on Erlang / OTP.</li>
<li aria-level="1">Simon Thompson is a professor of Logic and Computation at the University of Kent. He has been a teacher and researcher in functional programming for most of his career.</li>
</ul>

<h2 id="anchor-3">3. <a href="https://www.classcentral.com/course/independent-introduction-to-erlang-programming-120167" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Introduction to Erlang Programming (CodeRed)</a></h2>
<p><img loading="lazy" class="alignnone size-full wp-image-85271" src="https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2023/02/3.-Introduction-to-Erlang-Programming-CodeRed.png" alt="" width="1024" height="512" srcset="https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2023/02/3.-Introduction-to-Erlang-Programming-CodeRed.png 1024w, https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2023/02/3.-Introduction-to-Erlang-Programming-CodeRed-300x150.png 300w, https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2023/02/3.-Introduction-to-Erlang-Programming-CodeRed-768x384.png 768w" sizes="(max-width: 1024px) 100vw, 1024px" /></p>
<p>My third pick for the best Erlang course is <a href="https://www.classcentral.com/course/independent-introduction-to-erlang-programming-120167" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Introduction to Erlang Programming</a>.</p>
<p>This <b>paid </b>course is an excellent introduction for programmers looking to master the Erlang language. By the end, you’ll be able to build a system that uses functional concurrent programming to achieve scalability and reliability while still being easy to understand, debug, and maintain.</p>
<p>You’ll need basic programming knowledge and a MacOS or Linux system to take this course.</p>
<h3>What You’ll Learn</h3>
<p>The course starts by introducing you to the Erlang Shell, where you can get hands-on experience with the language by evaluating expressions and compiling modules. Then, you’ll delve into the world of functional programming in Erlang, including concepts such as pattern-matching and recursion. You’ll see how these functional programming techniques can be combined with concurrent programming to take advantage of Erlang&#8217;s efficient concurrency model using message-passing processes.</p>
<p>Next, you’ll cover how to handle errors in your Erlang program, both sequentially and concurrently, to ensure that it can continue running smoothly even in the face of unexpected issues. You’ll also learn about OTP that provides a powerful library and tools for building distributed systems. Finally, the course explores modern Erlang development practices and introduces you to Rebar3, a popular build and package management tool for Erlang.</p>
<h3>How You’ll Learn</h3>
<p>This course is 4 hours long. You’ll learn by watching the lecture videos chapter-by-chapter, with each chapter ending with a summary.</p>

<h2 id="anchor-4">4. <a href="https://www.classcentral.com/course/independent-learn-you-some-erlang-120165" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Learn You Some Erlang for Great Good! (Frederic Trottier-Hebert)</a></h2>
<p><img loading="lazy" class="alignnone size-full wp-image-85272" src="https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2023/02/4.-Learn-You-Some-Erlang-for-Great-Good-Frederic-Trottier-Hebert.png" alt="" width="1024" height="512" srcset="https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2023/02/4.-Learn-You-Some-Erlang-for-Great-Good-Frederic-Trottier-Hebert.png 1024w, https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2023/02/4.-Learn-You-Some-Erlang-for-Great-Good-Frederic-Trottier-Hebert-300x150.png 300w, https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2023/02/4.-Learn-You-Some-Erlang-for-Great-Good-Frederic-Trottier-Hebert-768x384.png 768w" sizes="(max-width: 1024px) 100vw, 1024px" /></p>
<p><a href="https://www.classcentral.com/course/independent-learn-you-some-erlang-120165" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Learn You Some Erlang for Great Good!</a> is a <b>free</b> comprehensive text-based Erlang tutorial, based on another well-received tutorial of similar name, <a href="http://learnyouahaskell.com/" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Learn You a Haskell for Great Good!</a>.</p>
<p>It is for people who have basic knowledge of programming in imperative languages but are unfamiliar with functional programming. You’ll explore how Erlang is very pragmatic in its approach to functional programming, and how it results in robust, concurrent, distributed systems.</p>
<h3>What You’ll Learn</h3>
<p>You’ll start by exploring the basics of the language, like variables, data types, and conditional statements. And since the language follows the functional paradigm, you’ll learn how to solve problems the functional way, using concepts like recursion and higher order functions.</p>
<p>Next, you’ll delve into the concepts of concurrency in Erlang and learn how to use processes, message passing, and other techniques to build concurrent systems. You’ll also learn about OTP (Open Telecom Platform), a set of libraries and tools for building distributed and fault-tolerant systems in Erlang. And this fault-tolerance can only be resolved through smart error and exception handling.</p>
<p>Data structures and algorithms appear everywhere in software, and Erlang is no exception. You’ll use them to solve common problems. You’ll also learn about working with sockets and networking, along with event handlers and supervisors.</p>
<p>Finally, you’ll learn about testing and debugging in Erlang, including how to use tools such as EUnit to test your code and how to release and deploy Erlang applications.</p>
<h3>How You’ll Learn</h3>
<p>This tutorial consists of 36 chapters. You’ll learn by reading through the many chapters and implementing the code given in the course on your system.</p>

<h2 id="anchor-5">5. <a href="https://www.classcentral.com/course/independent-erlang-logo-an-erlang-course-120164" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Erlang University (erlang.org)</a></h2>
<p><img loading="lazy" class="alignnone size-full wp-image-85273" src="https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2023/02/5.-Erlang-University-erlang.org_.png" alt="" width="1024" height="512" srcset="https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2023/02/5.-Erlang-University-erlang.org_.png 1024w, https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2023/02/5.-Erlang-University-erlang.org_-300x150.png 300w, https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2023/02/5.-Erlang-University-erlang.org_-768x384.png 768w" sizes="(max-width: 1024px) 100vw, 1024px" /></p>
<p><a href="https://www.classcentral.com/course/independent-erlang-logo-an-erlang-course-120164" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Erlang University</a> is the official Erlang course from the Ericsson OTP Team. This <b>free</b> text-based course covers Erlang from its history, to the basics parts of Erlang as well as to the advanced.</p>
<p>However, this course is quite bare, so be sure to supplement this course with other courses, the <a href="https://erlang.org/course/exercises.html" target="_blank" rel="noopener">course’s own exercises</a>, and <a href="https://erlangforums.com/" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Erlang’s discussion forums</a>.</p>
<p>Programming experience is needed to take this course.</p>
<h3>What You’ll Learn</h3>
<p>This course is divided into 5 modules.</p>
<p>First, you’ll take a short look at the history of Erlang to understand and appreciate the motivations and design principles behind its creation. Then, you’ll start with the basics of sequential programming which follows the style of many other languages where code is run on a single thread. This will include learning basic programming concepts as well as Erlang’s functional programming capabilities.</p>
<p>Next, you’ll get to the exciting part of Erlang: concurrent programming. You’ll understand how to use processes, lightweight concurrent units of execution that can run alongside other processes. You’ll also learn how errors can propagate through processes and how to handle them when they occur. Lastly, the course ends by covering a few tricky topics and quirks in the Erlang language.</p>
<h3>How You’ll Learn</h3>
<p>According to the course description, this course will take 4 days to complete, but that can vary depending on your current skill. You’ll learn by reading through the course modules and completing the exercises to help you put into practice what you’ve learned.</p>

<h2 id="anchor-6">6. <a href="https://www.classcentral.com/course/udemy-modern-erlang-for-beginners-120163" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Modern Erlang for Beginners (Roberto Ostinelli)</a></h2>
<p><img loading="lazy" class="alignnone size-full wp-image-85274" src="https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2023/02/6.-Modern-Erlang-for-Beginners-Roberto-Ostinelli.png" alt="" width="1024" height="512" srcset="https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2023/02/6.-Modern-Erlang-for-Beginners-Roberto-Ostinelli.png 1024w, https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2023/02/6.-Modern-Erlang-for-Beginners-Roberto-Ostinelli-300x150.png 300w, https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2023/02/6.-Modern-Erlang-for-Beginners-Roberto-Ostinelli-768x384.png 768w" sizes="(max-width: 1024px) 100vw, 1024px" /></p>
<p><a href="https://www.classcentral.com/course/udemy-modern-erlang-for-beginners-120163" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Modern Erlang for Beginners</a> is a <b>paid </b>Udemy course that provides a simple and concise introduction to Erlang.</p>
<p>To take this course, you should have some experience with another programming language.</p>
<h3>What You’ll Learn</h3>
<p>You’ll begin by installing and setting up Erlang on your PC, using the IntelliJ IDE. Then, you’ll learn Erlang basics, especially how to think in Erlang, like variables, control structures, data types, and data structure, as well as taking a careful look at functions, guards, and patterns in the context of functional programming.</p>
<p>Erlang is known for its ability to handle concurrent processing, and you’ll learn how it achieves this through processes, messages, and other techniques to build distributed systems. To further illustrate these concepts, you’ll examine a real-world example of a bank system. Finally, you’ll explore how to improve the bank example using the tools and libraries provided by the Open Telecom Platform (OTP) and learn best practices for Erlang development.</p>
<h3>How You’ll Learn</h3>
<p>This course is 3–4 hours long. You’ll learn by watching the lecture videos, taking notes of the code examples, and completing the course exercises.</p>

<h3>Fun Facts</h3>
<ul>
<li aria-level="1">Roberto Ostinelli is an experienced software developer with over a decade of professional experience using Erlang. He provides training to developers on how to build massively scalable systems using Erlang and Elixir, with a focus on TDD and agile methodologies.</li>
</ul>
<p>If you&#8217;re interested in this course, you can find <a href="https://www.classcentral.com/course/udemy-modern-erlang-for-beginners-120163" target="_blank" rel="noopener">more information about the course and how to enroll here</a>.</p>
<h2 id="anchor-7">7. <a href="https://www.classcentral.com/course/exercism-erlang-110593" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Erlang (Exercism)</a></h2>
<p><img loading="lazy" class="alignnone size-full wp-image-85275" src="https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2023/02/7.-Erlang-Exercism.png" alt="" width="1024" height="512" srcset="https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2023/02/7.-Erlang-Exercism.png 1024w, https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2023/02/7.-Erlang-Exercism-300x150.png 300w, https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2023/02/7.-Erlang-Exercism-768x384.png 768w" sizes="(max-width: 1024px) 100vw, 1024px" /></p>
<p><a href="https://www.classcentral.com/course/exercism-erlang-110593" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Exercism</a> is an excellent resource for improving your coding skills in Erlang. It is a <b>free </b>online coding platform that not only offers a variety of programming challenges and exercises for all skill levels, but it also provides a <b>free </b>mentoring service where you can request personalized feedback from experienced Erlang programmers for a particularly challenging exercise.</p>
<h3>What You’ll Learn</h3>
<p>The course consists of three difficulties: easy, medium, and hard.</p>
<p>Easy exercises consist of tasks like determining the geometric type of a triangle, finding the prime factors of a number, and implementing basic lists operations.</p>
<p>For medium difficulty exercises, you’ll calculate the date of meetups, add numbers to a  minesweeper board, and detect saddle points in a matrix.</p>
<p>Hard exercises include creating a zipper for a binary tree, returning a square matrix of a number in spiral order, and making a chain of dominoes.</p>
<h3>How You’ll Learn</h3>
<p>This course is self-paced, so you can take all the time you need to complete the 70+ hands-on programming exercises. Each exercise comes with automatic feedback of your code as well as personal mentoring to help you understand your code’s strengths and flaws.</p>

<h3>Fun Facts</h3>
<ul>
<li aria-level="1">Exercism provides exercises on 50+ programming languages like Python, Kotlin, F#, and even WebAssembly.</li>
<li aria-level="1">Their mission is to help everyone get really good at programming, regardless of their background, share the love of programming, and help people upskill as part of their upward social mobility.</li>
<li aria-level="1">Around 60 people have contributed towards the Erlang syllabus and exercises, with over 60 mentors available at the time of writing.</li>
</ul>
<p>If you&#8217;re interested in this course, you can find <a href="https://www.classcentral.com/course/exercism-erlang-110593" target="_blank" rel="noopener">more information about the course and how to enroll here</a>.</p>

		<title>Harvard CS50 Guide: How to Pick the Right Course (with Free Certificate)</title>
		<link>https://www.classcentral.com/report/harvard-cs50-guide/</link>
					<comments>https://www.classcentral.com/report/harvard-cs50-guide/#comments</comments>
		
		<dc:creator><![CDATA[Manoel Cortes Mendez]]></dc:creator>
		<pubDate>Tue, 07 Feb 2023 13:30:29 +0000</pubDate>
				<category><![CDATA[Guides]]></category>

					<description><![CDATA[<p>In 2023, Harvard CS50 offers 9 free certificate courses on topics such as computer science, Python, and AI.</p>
<p>The post <a rel="nofollow" href="https://www.classcentral.com/report/harvard-cs50-guide/">Harvard CS50 Guide: How to Pick the Right Course (with Free Certificate)</a> appeared first on <a rel="nofollow" href="https://www.classcentral.com/report">The Report by Class Central</a>.</p>
]]></description>
										<content:encoded><![CDATA[<figure id="attachment_85125" aria-describedby="caption-attachment-85125" style="width: 643px" class="wp-caption alignnone"><a href="https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2022/02/harvard-certificate.png"><img loading="lazy" class="wp-image-85125 size-full" src="https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2022/02/harvard-certificate.png" alt="" width="643" height="464" srcset="https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2022/02/harvard-certificate.png 643w, https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2022/02/harvard-certificate-300x216.png 300w" sizes="(max-width: 643px) 100vw, 643px" /></a><figcaption id="caption-attachment-85125" class="wp-caption-text">Harvard&#8217;s CS50 free certificate</figcaption></figure>
<p>In this article, I go over Harvard CS50&#8217;s entire course lineup, which in 2023 includes 11 courses — 9 of them with a free certificate of completion.</p>
<p>The CS50 adventure <a href="https://www.harvardmagazine.com/2012/11/classroom-in-the-cloud">began in 2012</a> with the launch of <a href="https://www.classcentral.com/course/edx-cs50-s-introduction-to-computer-science-442">CS50, Harvard&#8217;s Introduction to Computer Science</a>. Over the years, CS50 grew into a brand encompassing 10 additional courses on topics such as <a href="https://www.classcentral.com/report/harvard-cs50-python/">Python</a>, <a href="https://www.classcentral.com/course/edx-cs50-s-web-programming-with-python-and-javascript-11506">web development</a>, and <a href="https://www.classcentral.com/course/edx-cs50-s-introduction-to-artificial-intelligence-with-python-18122">AI</a>.</p>
<p>Let&#8217;s discuss the CS50 lineup, course by course, to help you find the best course for you. And let&#8217;s explain how you can earn a free certificate in most of these courses.</p>
<h2>CS50: The Original Course</h2>
<p>CS50 is taught by Harvard Professor <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/David_J._Malan">David J. Malan</a>. Back in 2015, when <a href="https://www.classcentral.com/">Class Central</a> contributor Charlie Soliman <a href="https://www.classcentral.com/report/review-david-malan-cs50-introduction-to-cs/">reviewed the course</a>, she said this about Professor Malan:</p>
<blockquote><p><em>At the risk of stating a cliché, his approach to teaching is unlike anything I have seen and can easily be labeled as revolutionary. One can detect the joy and effort he puts into each of his lectures.</em></p></blockquote>
<p>Having taken the course myself, I can say that this quote is as relevant today as it was back then. In fact, since the course is updated every year, the content has even gotten better. If you&#8217;d like to learn more, I&#8217;ve written a dedicated article on the course: <a href="https://www.classcentral.com/report/cs50-free-certificate/">Harvard CS50 in 2023: How to Get a Free Certificate</a>.</p>
<figure id="attachment_84535" aria-describedby="caption-attachment-84535" style="width: 919px" class="wp-caption alignnone"><a href="https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2022/05/cs50-2023-banner-e1673610020393.png"><img loading="lazy" class="wp-image-84535 size-full" src="https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2022/05/cs50-2023-banner-e1673610020393.png" alt="" width="919" height="458" srcset="https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2022/05/cs50-2023-banner-e1673610020393.png 919w, https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2022/05/cs50-2023-banner-e1673610020393-300x150.png 300w, https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2022/05/cs50-2023-banner-e1673610020393-768x383.png 768w" sizes="(max-width: 919px) 100vw, 919px" /></a><figcaption id="caption-attachment-84535" class="wp-caption-text">CS50 in Harvard&#8217;s Sanders Theater</figcaption></figure>
<p>Offered at <a href="https://www.thecrimson.com/article/2014/9/18/this-is-cs50/">Harvard since 2007</a> and on <a href="https://harvardmagazine.com/2012/11/classroom-in-the-cloud">edX since 2012</a>, CS50 has grown to become Harvard’s <a href="https://sites.duke.edu/csedpodcast/2019/12/23/episode-1-david-malan/">largest on-campus course</a>, with around 1000 students enrolled every Fall, and one of the world&#8217;s <a href="https://www.classcentral.com/report/top-moocs-2021-edition/">highest rated</a> and <a href="https://www.classcentral.com/report/most-popular-online-courses/">most popular</a> online courses ever, totalling over 4.3M enrollments.</p>
<p>And “CS50” has evolved from a code designating a <a href="https://www.classcentral.com/course/edx-cs50-s-introduction-to-computer-science-442">single course</a> to a brand encompassing <a href="https://www.classcentral.com/report/harvard-cs50-new-courses/">multiple courses</a> exploring different subjects, targeting different audiences, and part of different learning paths.</p>
<p>To make sense of Harvard CS50’s offering, I partly audited each course, I explored their online communities, and I contacted their course staff. I found that Professor Malan often replies to emails himself — a nice touch considering the course has over 100 staff. As CS50 keeps growing, I&#8217;ll continue to update this article.</p>
<h2>CS50: The Expanded Offering</h2>
<p>CS50’s full offering comprises 11 courses that can be broken down into 3 levels, as shown below. As you can see, 9 courses offer a free certificate. Click on a course or level to jump to the corresponding section.</p>

<h3 id="basic">Basic Courses</h3>
<p>Currently, CS50 offers two basic courses. These can be seen as optional on-ramps to CS50’s core courses. If you don’t feel ready for a formal introduction to computer science, this is a good place to start.</p>
<h4 id="CS50T"><a href="https://www.classcentral.com/course/edx-cs50-s-understanding-technology-10142">CS50&#8217;s Understanding Technology (CS50T)</a></h4>
<p><a href="https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2020/05/Screenshot-from-2020-05-19-18-28-41.png"><img loading="lazy" class="wp-image-71606 size-large" src="https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2020/05/Screenshot-from-2020-05-19-18-28-41-e1589907389429-1024x481.png" alt="CS50’s Understanding Technology" width="1024" height="481" srcset="https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2020/05/Screenshot-from-2020-05-19-18-28-41-e1589907389429-1024x481.png 1024w, https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2020/05/Screenshot-from-2020-05-19-18-28-41-e1589907389429-300x141.png 300w, https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2020/05/Screenshot-from-2020-05-19-18-28-41-e1589907389429-768x361.png 768w, https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2020/05/Screenshot-from-2020-05-19-18-28-41-e1589907389429-1536x722.png 1536w, https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2020/05/Screenshot-from-2020-05-19-18-28-41-e1589907389429.png 1920w" sizes="(max-width: 1024px) 100vw, 1024px" /></a></p>
<p>CS50T is a gentle introduction to the world of computing. It starts at the hardware level and works its way up from there. It explores how the internet works, how websites are created, and how security is ensured. And it ends with coding basics.</p>
<p>The course is taught by David J. Malan. It involves about 4 hours of study per week over 6 weeks. And it offers the following certificate options:</p>
<ul>
<li><a href="https://cs50.harvard.edu/technology">Free certificate</a> via Harvard OpenCourseWare</li>
<li><a href="https://www.classcentral.com/course/edx-cs50-s-understanding-technology-10142">Paid verified certificate</a> via edX</li>
<li><a href="https://web.dce.harvard.edu/extension/csci/e/1a">Paid transcript and academic credit</a> via Harvard Extension School</li>
</ul>
<p>The course is also part of edX&#8217;s <a href="https://www.classcentral.com/course/harvardx-cs50-ap-computer-science-principles-21947">XSeries program in CS50&#8217;s AP Computer Science Principles</a>.</p>
<h4 id="CS50S"><a href="https://www.classcentral.com/course/cs50s-introduction-to-programming-with-scratch-39309">CS50&#8217;s Introduction to Programming with Scratch (CS50S)</a></h4>
<p><a href="https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2020/05/cs50s.png"><img loading="lazy" class="alignnone wp-image-76346 size-full" src="https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2020/05/cs50s.png" alt="" width="1024" height="481" srcset="https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2020/05/cs50s.png 1024w, https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2020/05/cs50s-300x141.png 300w, https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2020/05/cs50s-768x361.png 768w" sizes="(max-width: 1024px) 100vw, 1024px" /></a></p>
<p>CS50S is a gentle introduction to programming. It focuses on Scratch, a language that makes coding highly visual. Instead of typing text, you combine functional blocks as if they were LEGO pieces to create programs. The course covers all programming fundamentals, including variables, functions, and loops.</p>
<p>The course is taught by <a href="https://brianyu.me/">Brian Yu</a>. It involves about 6 hours of study per week over 3 weeks. And it offers the following certificate options:</p>
<ul>
<li><a href="https://cs50.harvard.edu/scratch/">Free certificate</a> via Harvard OpenCourseWare</li>
<li><a href="https://www.classcentral.com/course/cs50s-introduction-to-programming-with-scratch-39309">Paid verified certificate</a> via edX</li>
</ul>
<h3 id="core">Core Courses</h3>
<p>Currently, CS50 offers three core courses. These include the original CS50 as well as variants geared toward different types of learners. This is where most learners want to start. One course should be plenty. But learners that take a variant may want to also take the original CS50 — especially if they plan to continue with a follow-up course.</p>
<h4 id="CS50"><a href="https://www.classcentral.com/course/edx-cs50-s-introduction-to-computer-science-442">CS50 Introduction to Computer Science</a></h4>
<p><a href="https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2022/05/cs50-2023-student-demo.png"><img loading="lazy" class="size-full wp-image-84537" src="https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2022/05/cs50-2023-student-demo.png" alt="" width="1024" height="512" srcset="https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2022/05/cs50-2023-student-demo.png 1024w, https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2022/05/cs50-2023-student-demo-300x150.png 300w, https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2022/05/cs50-2023-student-demo-768x384.png 768w" sizes="(max-width: 1024px) 100vw, 1024px" /></a></p>
<p>CS50 is Harvard’s computer science introduction. It starts with binary and goes up the ladder of abstraction from machine code to low-level languages to high-level languages. It explores algorithms, data structures, and memory management. And it ends with one of three specialization tracks: web, game, or mobile development.</p>
<p>The course is taught by David J. Malan. It involves about 12 hours of study per week over 12 weeks. And it offers the following certificate options:</p>
<ul>
<li><a href="https://cs50.harvard.edu/x">Free certificate</a> via Harvard OpenCourseWare</li>
<li><a href="https://www.classcentral.com/course/edx-cs50-s-introduction-to-computer-science-442">Paid verified certificate</a> via edX</li>
<li>Paid transcript and academic credit via <a href="https://web.dce.harvard.edu/extension/csci/e/50">Harvard Extension School</a> or <a href="https://web.dce.harvard.edu/summer/csci/s/50">Harvard Summer School</a></li>
</ul>
<p>The course is also part of edX&#8217;s professional certificates:</p>
<ul>
<li><a href="https://www.classcentral.com/course/harvardx-computer-science-for-web-programming-18465">Computer Science for Web Programming</a></li>
<li><a href="https://www.classcentral.com/course/harvardx-computer-science-for-artifical-intellige-18468">Computer Science for Artificial Intelligence</a></li>
<li><a href="https://www.classcentral.com/course/harvardx-computer-science-for-game-development-18456">Computer Science for Game Development</a></li>
</ul>
<p>If you&#8217;d like to learn more, I&#8217;ve written a dedicated article on the course: <a href="https://www.classcentral.com/report/cs50-free-certificate/">Harvard CS50 in 2023: How to Get a Free Certificate</a>.</p>
<h4 id="CS50L"><a href="https://www.classcentral.com/course/edx-cs50-for-lawyers-16857">CS50’s Computer Science for Lawyers (CS50L)</a></h4>
<p><a href="https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2020/05/cs50lawfinal.png"><img loading="lazy" class="alignnone size-large wp-image-71611" src="https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2020/05/cs50lawfinal-1024x479.png" alt="CS50 for lawyers" width="1024" height="479" srcset="https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2020/05/cs50lawfinal-1024x479.png 1024w, https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2020/05/cs50lawfinal-300x140.png 300w, https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2020/05/cs50lawfinal-768x359.png 768w, https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2020/05/cs50lawfinal.png 1180w" sizes="(max-width: 1024px) 100vw, 1024px" /></a></p>
<p>CS50L is a CS50 variant geared toward lawyers and law students. Part of the curriculum explores similar content but emphasizes big-picture understanding over low-level details. The other part explores entirely new content that considers how law and computer science interact — for instance, in regards to cybersecurity, data privacy, and internet regulation.</p>
<p>The course is taught by David J. Malan and <a href="https://douglloyd.com/">Doug Lloyd</a>. It involves about 4 hours of study per week over 10 weeks. And it offers the following certificate options:</p>
<ul>
<li><a href="https://cs50.harvard.edu/law/">Free certificate</a> via Harvard OpenCourseWare</li>
<li><a href="https://www.classcentral.com/course/edx-cs50-for-lawyers-16857">Paid verified certificate</a> via edX</li>
<li><a href="https://hls.harvard.edu/executive-education/programs/online-programs/computer-science-for-lawyers/">Paid certificate</a> via Harvard Law School Executive Education</li>
</ul>
<h4 id="CS50B"><a href="https://www.classcentral.com/course/edx-cs50-s-computer-science-for-business-professionals-10143">CS50&#8217;s Computer Science for Business Professionals (CS50B)</a></h4>
<p><a href="https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2020/05/cs50b.png"><img loading="lazy" class="alignnone wp-image-71610 size-large" src="https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2020/05/cs50b-e1589908163415-1024x478.png" alt="CS50 Business" width="1024" height="478" srcset="https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2020/05/cs50b-e1589908163415-1024x478.png 1024w, https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2020/05/cs50b-e1589908163415-300x140.png 300w, https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2020/05/cs50b-e1589908163415-768x359.png 768w, https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2020/05/cs50b-e1589908163415-1536x718.png 1536w, https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2020/05/cs50b-e1589908163415.png 1920w" sizes="(max-width: 1024px) 100vw, 1024px" /></a></p>
<p>CS50B is a CS50 variant geared toward business professionals. Most of the course explores similar content but emphasizes big-picture understanding over low-level details. A small part explores entirely new content relevant to businesses — for instance, cloud computing.</p>
<p>The course is taught by David J. Malan. It involves about 4 hours of study per week over 6 weeks. And it offers the following certificate options:</p>
<ul>
<li><a href="https://cs50.harvard.edu/business/">Free certificate</a> via Harvard OpenCourseWare</li>
<li><a href="https://www.classcentral.com/course/edx-cs50-s-computer-science-for-business-professionals-10143">Paid verified certificate</a> via edX</li>
<li>Paid transcript and academic credit via <a href="https://web.dce.harvard.edu/extension/csci/e/1b">Harvard Extension School</a> or <a href="https://web.dce.harvard.edu/summer/csci/s/1b">Harvard Summer School</a></li>
</ul>
<h4 id="CS50P"><a href="https://www.classcentral.com/course/cs50s-introduction-to-programming-with-python-58275">CS50&#8217;s Introduction to Programming with Python (CS50P)</a></h4>
<p><a href="https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2021/09/cs50-python.png"><img loading="lazy" class="alignnone size-full wp-image-78729" src="https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2021/09/cs50-python.png" alt="" width="1024" height="478" srcset="https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2021/09/cs50-python.png 1024w, https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2021/09/cs50-python-300x140.png 300w, https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2021/09/cs50-python-768x359.png 768w" sizes="(max-width: 1024px) 100vw, 1024px" /></a></p>
<p>CS50P teaches the fundamentals of programming in Python, including variables, functions, loops, and reading and writing files. It draws from real-world programming problems and has plenty of practical exercises.</p>
<p>The course is taught by David J. Malan. It involves about 6 hours of study per week over 9 weeks. And it offers the following certificate options:</p>
<ul>
<li><a href="https://cs50.harvard.edu/python">Free certificate</a> via Harvard OpenCourseWare</li>
<li><a href="https://www.classcentral.com/course/cs50s-introduction-to-programming-with-python-58275">Paid verified certificate</a> via edX</li>
<li><a href="https://courses.dce.harvard.edu/?details&amp;srcdb=202301&amp;crn=15376">Paid transcript and academic credit</a> via Harvard Extension School (taught by Jeff Parker)</li>
</ul>
<p>The course is also part of edX&#8217;s <a href="https://www.classcentral.com/course/harvardx-computer-science-for-python-programming-98208">Professional Certificate in Computer Science for Python Programming</a>.</p>
<p>If you&#8217;d like to learn more, I&#8217;ve written a dedicated article on the course: <a href="https://www.classcentral.com/report/harvard-cs50-python/">Harvard New Intro to Python: How to Earn a Free Certificate</a>.</p>
<h3 id="followup">Follow-Up Courses</h3>
<p>Currently, CS50 offers five follow-up courses. These pick up where CS50 leaves off and explore a specific subject. They&#8217;re an excellent way to build on your computer science fundamentals by delving into a specialization.</p>
<h4 id="CS50AI"><a href="https://www.classcentral.com/course/edx-cs50-s-introduction-to-artificial-intelligence-with-python-18122">CS50’s Introduction to Artificial Intelligence with Python (CS50AI)</a></h4>
<p><a href="https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2020/05/cs50ai.png"><img loading="lazy" class="alignnone wp-image-71612 size-large" src="https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2020/05/cs50ai-e1589908343841-1024x478.png" alt="CS50 AI" width="1024" height="478" srcset="https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2020/05/cs50ai-e1589908343841-1024x478.png 1024w, https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2020/05/cs50ai-e1589908343841-300x140.png 300w, https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2020/05/cs50ai-e1589908343841-768x359.png 768w, https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2020/05/cs50ai-e1589908343841-1536x718.png 1536w, https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2020/05/cs50ai-e1589908343841.png 1920w" sizes="(max-width: 1024px) 100vw, 1024px" /></a></p>
<p>CS50AI leverages the Python programming language to explore modern artificial intelligence. It covers foundational AI concepts, such as search algorithms and knowledge models, and builds on them to discuss more advanced concepts, such as optimization and machine learning.</p>
<p>The course is taught by <a href="https://brianyu.me/">Brian Yu</a>. It involves about 20 hours of study per week over 7 weeks. And it offers the following certificate options:</p>
<ul>

<li><a href="https://www.classcentral.com/course/edx-cs50-s-introduction-to-artificial-intelligence-with-python-18122">Paid verified certificate</a> via edX</li>

</ul>

<p>CS50W explores the languages, tools, and processes underpinning modern web app development. It covers languages such as Python and JavaScript, frameworks such as Flask and Django, and services such as GitHub and Heroku.</p>

<h2>What are CSS Animations?</h2>
<p>CSS animations is a proposed module for Cascading Style Sheets that allows the animation of HTML document elements using CSS.</p>
<h3>Why should you learn CSS Animations when you can create animations using javascript?</h3>
<p>CSS Animations are preferred over JavaScript in for several reasons such as:</p>
<ol>
<li aria-level="1">Performance: CSS Animations are typically smoother and faster than JavaScript animations because they are hardware-accelerated and run on the browser&#8217;s compositor thread, rather than the main JavaScript thread.</li>
<li aria-level="1">Simplicity: CSS Animations are generally simpler to implement and maintain than JavaScript animations. With CSS, you can animate elements with a few lines of code, whereas JavaScript animations require more complex logic and code.</li>
<li aria-level="1">Accessibility: CSS Animations can be controlled with CSS and are accessible to users with assistive technologies, such as screen readers. JavaScript animations, on the other hand, may not be accessible to all users.</li>
<li aria-level="1">Browser support: CSS Animations have good browser support, meaning they work on most modern browsers. This is not always the case with JavaScript animations, as some browsers may not support certain JavaScript features.</li>
</ol>
<p>So, let’s learn some Animation with CSS.</p>
<p><a href="https://www.classcentral.com/" target="_blank" rel="noopener"><img loading="lazy" class="alignnone wp-image-79247 size-full" src="https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2022/03/Class-Central-Preview-1.png" alt="Find your next course." width="1024" height="512" srcset="https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2022/03/Class-Central-Preview-1.png 1024w, https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2022/03/Class-Central-Preview-1-300x150.png 300w, https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2022/03/Class-Central-Preview-1-768x384.png 768w" sizes="(max-width: 1024px) 100vw, 1024px" /></a></p>
<h2>Best Courses Guides Methodology</h2>
<p>I built this ranking following the now tried-and-tested methodology used in previous Best Courses Guides (<a href="https://www.classcentral.com/report/category/best-courses/" target="_blank" rel="noopener">you can find them all here</a>). It involves a three-step process:</p>
<ol>
<li aria-level="1"><b>Research:</b> I started by leveraging Class Central’s database with <a href="https://www.classcentral.com/subjects" target="_blank" rel="noopener">100K online courses</a> and 200K+ reviews. Then, I made a preliminary selection of 40 courses by rating, reviews, and bookmarks.</li>
<li aria-level="1"><b>Evaluate:</b> I read through reviews on Class Central, Reddit, and course providers to understand what other learners thought about each course and combined it with my own experience as a <a href="https://www.classcentral.com/@kinjalvora" target="_blank" rel="noopener">learner</a>.</li>
<li aria-level="1"><b>Select:</b> Well-made courses were picked if they presented valuable and engaging content and they have to fit in a set of criteria and be ranked accordingly: comprehensive curriculum, affordability, release date, ratings and enrollments.</li>
</ol>
<h2>Course Ranking Statistics</h2>
<p>Here are some aggregate stats about the ranking:</p>
<ul>
<li aria-level="1">Over 15k people are following <a href="https://www.classcentral.com/subject/html-css" target="_blank" rel="noopener">HTML and CSS</a> on Class Central.</li>
<li aria-level="1">All of the courses in this ranking require a basic knowledge of HTML/CSS.</li>
<li aria-level="1">7 of the courses in this ranking are <b>free</b>, <b>free-to-audit</b>, or have <b>free-trial</b>, whereas the rest are paid.</li>
<li aria-level="1">Most of the courses are suitable for CSS-Animation beginners.</li>
</ul>
<p>Without further ado, let’s go through the top picks.</p>
<h2 id="anchor-1">1. <a href="https://www.classcentral.com/course/independent-css-animations-126055" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Hello Animation (HTML Academy)</a></h2>
<p><img loading="lazy" class="alignnone wp-image-85204 size-full" src="https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2023/02/1.-Hello-Animation-HTML-Academy.png" alt="" width="1024" height="512" srcset="https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2023/02/1.-Hello-Animation-HTML-Academy.png 1024w, https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2023/02/1.-Hello-Animation-HTML-Academy-300x150.png 300w, https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2023/02/1.-Hello-Animation-HTML-Academy-768x384.png 768w" sizes="(max-width: 1024px) 100vw, 1024px" /></p>
<p>My first pick is the <a href="https://www.classcentral.com/course/independent-css-animations-126055" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Hello Animation</a> course offered for <b>free</b> by HTML Academy. The course is a mix of theory and practice. You start with some basic animation and then handle animations of multiple objects simultaneously using keyframes.</p>
<p>By the end of this course you will be familiar with keyframes and creating basic and even some complex animations.</p>
<h3>What You’ll Learn</h3>
<p>You will learn to rotate, slide, transform simple objects and even send a rocket to space. The course will get you acquainted with keyframes, pre and post animation states and animation timing with 32 practice tutorials.</p>
<h3>How You’ll Learn</h3>
<p>There is a theoretical side and a practical side to the course, you will first be given some theory to understand the concepts and then move to practicing what you have read in the theory. There are 32 hands-on exercises to get you familiarized with the basics of CSS Animation.</p>
<table>
