<h2 id="anchor-2">2. <a href="https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=LCEgHntqBps" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Learn CSS Animation with Jad Khalili (Scrimba)</a></h2>
<p><img loading="lazy" class="alignnone wp-image-85205 size-full" src="https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2023/02/2.-Learn-CSS-Animation-with-Jad-Khalili-Scrimba.png" alt="" width="1024" height="512" srcset="https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2023/02/2.-Learn-CSS-Animation-with-Jad-Khalili-Scrimba.png 1024w, https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2023/02/2.-Learn-CSS-Animation-with-Jad-Khalili-Scrimba-300x150.png 300w, https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2023/02/2.-Learn-CSS-Animation-with-Jad-Khalili-Scrimba-768x384.png 768w" sizes="(max-width: 1024px) 100vw, 1024px" /></p>
<p>This is a pro course offered by Scrimba. <a href="https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=LCEgHntqBps" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Learn CSS Animation with Jad Khalili</a> is available for free on youtube. You will learn CSS Animation by solving real-world problems when doing front-end development.</p>
<p>The course covers various techniques for adding transitions and customizing them, as well as how to define animations and control timing. The course also teaches different types of transforms, including scaling, translation, rotation, and skew, and how to apply them to elements. Additionally, it covers the use of CSS variables and timing functions to control animation behavior. It also covers the use of prefixes to ensure cross-browser compatibility. You will be able to test and review all that you have learnt in the course with some real world challenges.</p>
<h3>What You’ll Learn</h3>
<p>The course will teach you transitions, customizing transitions and working on a real world transition challenge. It will then proceed to explain animations and timings in animation with another real world challenge. The last challenge would be to work on a logo with transformations and translations and creating custom timing functions.</p>
<h3>How You’ll Learn</h3>
<p>You will learn by watching the video and following the material with the instructor.</p>

<h2 id="anchor-5">5. <a href="https://www.classcentral.com/course/linkedin-learning-css-animation-99982" target="_blank" rel="noopener">CSS: Animation (Val Head)</a></h2>
<p><img loading="lazy" class="alignnone size-full wp-image-85208" src="https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2023/02/5.-CSS_-Animation-Val-Head.png" alt="" width="1024" height="512" srcset="https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2023/02/5.-CSS_-Animation-Val-Head.png 1024w, https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2023/02/5.-CSS_-Animation-Val-Head-300x150.png 300w, https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2023/02/5.-CSS_-Animation-Val-Head-768x384.png 768w" sizes="(max-width: 1024px) 100vw, 1024px" /></p>
<p><a href="https://www.classcentral.com/course/linkedin-learning-css-animation-99982" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Val Head’s <b>free</b> course</a> on Linkedin Learning is one of the first courses in the list to introduce SVG Animation using CSS. You shall get acquainted with CSS Animation but also get to understand some Vector Graphics through the course.</p>
<h3>What You’ll Learn</h3>
<p>This course includes information on using CSS transforms and transitions, working with animation-delay and animation-fill-mode, and timing and easing CSS animations. The course also covers animating elements in place, animating sprite images, chaining multiple animations, and animating SVG images. Additionally, it discusses strategies for creating high-performance CSS animations and how to optimize them to ensure smooth performance.</p>
<h3>How You’ll Learn</h3>
<p>Val introduces CSS transforms and transitions—the foundation of most CSS animations—and shows how to keyframe simple animations and adjust their timing, fill-mode, and direction. She also covers looping and chaining animations, animating HTML and SVG elements, optimizing animation performance, best uses for CSS animations right now, and the current level of support and performance and how we can expect that to change in the future. Val presents the lessons as a short series of building block animations—common things you might want to do with animations—then puts those techniques together in a small project of an animated infographic so you can see them all in action.</p>

</ul>

		<title>Massive List of Chinese Online Course Platforms in 2023</title>
		<link>https://www.classcentral.com/report/chinese-mooc-platforms/</link>
					<comments>https://www.classcentral.com/report/chinese-mooc-platforms/#comments</comments>
		
		<dc:creator><![CDATA[Rui Ma]]></dc:creator>
		<pubDate>Mon, 06 Feb 2023 13:45:13 +0000</pubDate>
				<category><![CDATA[Guides]]></category>

					<description><![CDATA[<p>Online education is alive and well in China. Combined, these platforms offer over 100K online courses.</p>
<p>The post <a rel="nofollow" href="https://www.classcentral.com/report/chinese-mooc-platforms/">Massive List of Chinese Online Course Platforms in 2023</a> appeared first on <a rel="nofollow" href="https://www.classcentral.com/report">The Report by Class Central</a>.</p>
]]></description>
										<content:encoded><![CDATA[<p><img loading="lazy" class="alignnone wp-image-73877 size-full" src="https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2021/01/chinese-lang-platforms.png" alt="Chinese Language MOOC Platforms" width="1024" height="512" srcset="https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2021/01/chinese-lang-platforms.png 1024w, https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2021/01/chinese-lang-platforms-300x150.png 300w, https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2021/01/chinese-lang-platforms-768x384.png 768w" sizes="(max-width: 1024px) 100vw, 1024px" /></p>
<p>The origins of <a href="https://www.classcentral.com/help/moocs" target="_blank" rel="noopener">massive open online courses</a> (MOOCs) in China can be traced back to <a href="https://pdfs.semanticscholar.org/07ff/a996d12fff4691ead559912a41cdf31d54b3.pdf" target="_blank" rel="noopener">November 2011</a>, when <a href="http://www.chinadaily.com.cn/cndy/2011-11/10/content_14068582.htm" target="_blank" rel="noopener">20 courses</a> from Chinese universities were made available online through the <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/OpenCourseWare" target="_blank" rel="noopener">OpenCourseWare</a> platform <a href="http://www.icourses.cn/home/" target="_blank" rel="noopener">iCourse</a>.</p>
<p>For years at <a href="https://www.classcentral.com/">Class Central</a>, we&#8217;ve been interested in the development of online education in China. You can find our <a href="https://www.classcentral.com/report/tag/china/">coverage on the subject here</a>.</p>
<p>In this article, we discuss the emergence of MOOCs in China and compile a comprehensive list of Chinese-language online course platforms.</p>
<h2>Origins</h2>
<p>The first full-fledged MOOC platform in China, <a href="https://www.classcentral.com/report/xuetangx/" target="_blank" rel="noopener">XuetangX</a>, was launched in October 2013 by <a href="https://www.classcentral.com/university/tsu" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Tsinghua University</a>. Many more similar platforms would promptly follow.</p>
<p>Like <a href="https://www.classcentral.com/report/mooc-platforms/" target="_blank" rel="noopener">online course platforms worldwide</a>, Chinese MOOC platforms saw a <a href="https://www.classcentral.com/report/the-second-year-of-the-mooc/" target="_blank" rel="noopener">surge</a> in both <a href="https://mp.weixin.qq.com/s/08dMP3NQXSqTXznRajBsmw" target="_blank" rel="noopener">course numbers and enrollments</a> in 2020 due to the pandemic.</p>
<p>In <strong>early 2022</strong>, the Chinese platforms listed in this article offered close to <strong>70K</strong> online courses. That&#8217;s about twice as many as in 2020. Now, in <strong>early 2023</strong>, we reached a total of about <strong>100K</strong> courses, showing that the growth trend perdures.</p>
<p>On March 28, 2022, China’s Ministry of Education announced the “<a href="https://www.classcentral.com/report/china-integrated-platforms/">Smart Education of China</a>” initiative and launched the comprehensive website <a href="https://www.chinaooc.com.cn/">Chinaooc</a>, bringing together all the MOOC platforms of mainland China.</p>
<h2>Platforms</h2>
<p>Here are the Chinese online course platforms that focus on MOOCs. You can click on one to jump to the description.</p>
<ul>
<li><a href="#XuetangX">XuetangX</a></li>

<li><a href="#OpenEdu">OpenEdu</a></li>
</ul>
<hr />
<h2 id="XuetangX">XuetangX</h2>
<figure id="attachment_85163" aria-describedby="caption-attachment-85163" style="width: 1536px" class="wp-caption alignnone"><a href="https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2022/01/xuetangx-homepage-2023-cropped.png"><img loading="lazy" class="size-full wp-image-85163" src="https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2022/01/xuetangx-homepage-2023-cropped.png" alt="" width="1536" height="854" srcset="https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2022/01/xuetangx-homepage-2023-cropped.png 1536w, https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2022/01/xuetangx-homepage-2023-cropped-300x167.png 300w, https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2022/01/xuetangx-homepage-2023-cropped-1024x569.png 1024w, https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2022/01/xuetangx-homepage-2023-cropped-768x427.png 768w" sizes="(max-width: 1536px) 100vw, 1536px" /></a><figcaption id="caption-attachment-85163" class="wp-caption-text"><a href="https://www.xuetangx.com/">XuetangX homepage</a> in 2023</figcaption></figure>
<p>In October 2013, <a href="https://www.classcentral.com/university/tsu" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Tsinghua University</a> along with partner institutions in China <a href="https://web.archive.org/web/20200804053937/https://www.edx.org/press/edx-open-source-platform-chosen-power" target="_blank" rel="noopener">announced</a> the launch of XuetangX, China’s first MOOC platform. The are close to <a href="https://www.xuetangx.com/search">7000 courses</a> and programs offered on the platform, including live streamings, online degrees, microcredentials, and cohort-based boot camps. XuetangX reached over <a href="https://mp.weixin.qq.com/s/an4guDM-tEFz4Vn7Bs_pZA" target="_blank" rel="noopener">80 million</a> users at its 8th anniversary on October 10, 2021.</p>
<p>The platform raised <a href="https://www.classcentral.com/report/xuetangx-raises-funding-drops-open-edx/" target="_blank" rel="noopener">series B funding</a>, moved away from Open edX and <a href="https://next.xuetangx.com/" target="_blank" rel="noopener">redesigned</a> their website at the beginning of 2020. In April 2020, <a href="https://www.classcentral.com/report/china-mooc-platforms-go-international/" target="_blank" rel="noopener">it went international</a> and began to offer around 470 free English courses for global learners.</p>
<p>Here&#8217;s some of Class Central&#8217;s previous coverage on XuetangX:</p>
<ul>
<li><a href="https://www.classcentral.com/report/xuetangx-raises-funding-drops-open-edx/" target="_blank" rel="noopener">XuetangX Raises Series B Funding, Moves Away From Open edX Platform</a></li>
<li><a href="https://www.classcentral.com/report/china-mooc-platforms-go-international/" target="_blank" rel="noopener">China’s Largest MOOC Platforms Go International, Launch Courses in English</a></li>
<li><a href="https://www.classcentral.com/report/xuetangx/" target="_blank" rel="noopener">XuetangX: A Look at China’s First and Biggest MOOC Platform</a></li>
</ul>
<h2 id="Chinese-University-MOOC">Chinese University MOOC</h2>
<figure id="attachment_85167" aria-describedby="caption-attachment-85167" style="width: 1536px" class="wp-caption alignnone"><a href="https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2022/01/icourse-homepage-2023-cropped-final.png"><img loading="lazy" class="size-full wp-image-85167" src="https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2022/01/icourse-homepage-2023-cropped-final.png" alt="" width="1536" height="767" srcset="https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2022/01/icourse-homepage-2023-cropped-final.png 1536w, https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2022/01/icourse-homepage-2023-cropped-final-300x150.png 300w, https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2022/01/icourse-homepage-2023-cropped-final-1024x511.png 1024w, https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2022/01/icourse-homepage-2023-cropped-final-768x384.png 768w" sizes="(max-width: 1536px) 100vw, 1536px" /></a><figcaption id="caption-attachment-85167" class="wp-caption-text"><a href="https://www.icourse163.org/">iCourse homepage</a> in 2023</figcaption></figure>
<p>Chinese University MOOC, also often called <a href="https://www.icourse163.org/">iCourse</a>, is the fruit of a collaboration between the Chinese internet giant NetEase and the original <a href="http://www.icourses.cn/home/" target="_blank" rel="noopener">iCourse learning platform</a>. The MOOC platform offers over 10,000 free university courses, including <a href="https://www.classcentral.com/report/china-national-moocs/" target="_blank" rel="noopener">nationally-recognized MOOCs</a>. Free digital certificates are automatically available when students pass quizzes and final exam.</p>
<h2 id="Zhihuishu">Zhihui Shu</h2>
<figure id="attachment_85169" aria-describedby="caption-attachment-85169" style="width: 1536px" class="wp-caption alignnone"><a href="https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2022/01/zhihuishu-homepage-2023.png"><img loading="lazy" class="wp-image-85169 size-full" src="https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2022/01/zhihuishu-homepage-2023.png" alt="" width="1536" height="791" srcset="https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2022/01/zhihuishu-homepage-2023.png 1536w, https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2022/01/zhihuishu-homepage-2023-300x154.png 300w, https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2022/01/zhihuishu-homepage-2023-1024x527.png 1024w, https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2022/01/zhihuishu-homepage-2023-768x396.png 768w" sizes="(max-width: 1536px) 100vw, 1536px" /></a><figcaption id="caption-attachment-85169" class="wp-caption-text"><a href="https://www.zhihuishu.com/">Zhihui Shu homepage</a> in 2023</figcaption></figure>
<p><a href="https://www.zhihuishu.com/">Zhihui Shu</a>, which translates to “Wisdom Tree”, was launched in <a href="https://www.google.com/books/edition/_/T5xBDwAAQBAJ?hl=en" target="_blank" rel="noopener">December 2012</a>. It has the particularity of allowing its university partners to share credit-bearing courses with one another, facilitating academic credit mobility across China.</p>
<p>Of the 14,100 courses offered on the platform, 10,500 (that is, 75%) are credit-granting courses only for on-campus students. The platform offers <a href="https://www.zhihuishu.com/portals_h5/2clearning.html#/courseResource/?type=3&amp;label=-1&amp;payState=0&amp;interestSort=1" target="_blank" rel="noopener">45</a> courses with a free digital certificates. And there are also <a href="https://www.zhihuishu.com/columnsapp/student/microSpecialtyMore.html" target="_blank" rel="noopener">18 microcredential programs</a> available.</p>
<h2 id="CNMOOC">CNMOOC</h2>
<figure id="attachment_85171" aria-describedby="caption-attachment-85171" style="width: 1536px" class="wp-caption alignnone"><a href="https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2022/01/CNMOOC-homepage-2023.png"><img loading="lazy" class="wp-image-85171 size-full" src="https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2022/01/CNMOOC-homepage-2023.png" alt="" width="1536" height="991" srcset="https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2022/01/CNMOOC-homepage-2023.png 1536w, https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2022/01/CNMOOC-homepage-2023-300x194.png 300w, https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2022/01/CNMOOC-homepage-2023-1024x661.png 1024w, https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2022/01/CNMOOC-homepage-2023-768x496.png 768w" sizes="(max-width: 1536px) 100vw, 1536px" /></a><figcaption id="caption-attachment-85171" class="wp-caption-text"><a href="https://www.cnmooc.org/">CNMOOC homepage</a> in 2023</figcaption></figure>
<p>In April 2014, Shanghai Jiao Tong University launched <a href="https://www.cnmooc.org/">CNMOOC</a>, a online course platform promoting the integration of MOOCs into China’s on-campus higher education system. The platform offers over <a href="https://www.cnmooc.org/portal/frontCourseIndex/course.mooc" target="_blank" rel="noopener">3000</a> courses. About half of them provide free digital certificates.</p>
<h2 id="Xue-Yin-Online">Xue Yin Online</h2>
<figure id="attachment_85172" aria-describedby="caption-attachment-85172" style="width: 1536px" class="wp-caption alignnone"><a href="https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2022/01/Xue-Yin-Online-homepage-2023.png"><img loading="lazy" class="wp-image-85172 size-full" src="https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2022/01/Xue-Yin-Online-homepage-2023.png" alt="" width="1536" height="698" srcset="https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2022/01/Xue-Yin-Online-homepage-2023.png 1536w, https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2022/01/Xue-Yin-Online-homepage-2023-300x136.png 300w, https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2022/01/Xue-Yin-Online-homepage-2023-1024x465.png 1024w, https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2022/01/Xue-Yin-Online-homepage-2023-768x349.png 768w" sizes="(max-width: 1536px) 100vw, 1536px" /></a><figcaption id="caption-attachment-85172" class="wp-caption-text"><a href="https://www.xueyinonline.com/">Xue Yin Online homepage</a> in 2023</figcaption></figure>
<p><a href="https://www.xueyinonline.com/">Xue Yin Online</a> launched in November 2017. It was developed by The Open University of China and the Chaoxing Group. The purpose of this online course platform is to serve as a “credit bank” for vocational skills, facilitating the transfer of credit and the recognition of prior learning across different universities. The platform offers nearly over <a href="http://www.xueyinonline.com/mooc/courselist" target="_blank" rel="noopener">16,000</a> course with a free digital certificate.</p>
<h2 id="Chinese-MOOCs">Chinese MOOCs</h2>
<figure id="attachment_85174" aria-describedby="caption-attachment-85174" style="width: 1536px" class="wp-caption alignnone"><a href="https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2022/01/chinese-moocs-homepage-2023.png"><img loading="lazy" class="wp-image-85174 size-full" src="https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2022/01/chinese-moocs-homepage-2023.png" alt="" width="1536" height="557" srcset="https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2022/01/chinese-moocs-homepage-2023.png 1536w, https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2022/01/chinese-moocs-homepage-2023-300x109.png 300w, https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2022/01/chinese-moocs-homepage-2023-1024x371.png 1024w, https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2022/01/chinese-moocs-homepage-2023-768x279.png 768w" sizes="(max-width: 1536px) 100vw, 1536px" /></a><figcaption id="caption-attachment-85174" class="wp-caption-text"><a href="http://www.chinesemooc.org/">Chinese MOOCs</a> homepage in 2023</figcaption></figure>
<p><a href="http://www.chinesemooc.org/">Chinese MOOCs</a> was founded in <a href="https://www.google.com/books/edition/_/T5xBDwAAQBAJ?hl=en" target="_blank" rel="noopener">February 2015</a> by Peking University in collaboration with the Alibaba Group. About <a href="http://www.chinesemooc.org/kvideo.php?do=search" target="_blank" rel="noopener">150 free courses</a> with a <a href="http://www.chinesemooc.org/do.php?ac=helpCenter" target="_blank" rel="noopener">free digital certificate</a> are offered on the platform, most of them provided by Peking University.</p>
<h2 id="UOOC-Online">UOOC Online</h2>
<figure id="attachment_85175" aria-describedby="caption-attachment-85175" style="width: 1536px" class="wp-caption alignnone"><a href="https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2022/01/uooc-online-homepage-2023.png"><img loading="lazy" class="wp-image-85175 size-full" src="https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2022/01/uooc-online-homepage-2023.png" alt="" width="1536" height="829" srcset="https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2022/01/uooc-online-homepage-2023.png 1536w, https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2022/01/uooc-online-homepage-2023-300x162.png 300w, https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2022/01/uooc-online-homepage-2023-1024x553.png 1024w, https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2022/01/uooc-online-homepage-2023-768x415.png 768w" sizes="(max-width: 1536px) 100vw, 1536px" /></a><figcaption id="caption-attachment-85175" class="wp-caption-text"><a href="http://www.uooconline.com/">UOOC homepage</a> in 2023</figcaption></figure>
<p>The <a href="http://www.uooconline.com/">University Open Online Courses</a> (UOOC) platform was founded by Shenzhen University in February 2016, subsuming the preexisting MOOC platform from <a href="http://www.suda.edu.cn/eng/News/SoochowNews/201611/AE0FB5A2-FBE4-4116-85BE-A14E3FE2307E.html" target="_blank" rel="noopener">April 2014</a>. The are <a href="http://www.uooconline.com/course/list" target="_blank" rel="noopener">1375</a> free courses on the platform, with the vast majority also offering credit for on-campus students.</p>
<h2 id="Zhejiang-Provincial-MOOC-Platform">Zhejiang Provincial MOOC Platform</h2>
<figure id="attachment_85176" aria-describedby="caption-attachment-85176" style="width: 1536px" class="wp-caption alignnone"><a href="https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2022/01/Zhejiang-online-homepage-2023.png"><img loading="lazy" class="wp-image-85176 size-full" src="https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2022/01/Zhejiang-online-homepage-2023.png" alt="" width="1536" height="797" srcset="https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2022/01/Zhejiang-online-homepage-2023.png 1536w, https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2022/01/Zhejiang-online-homepage-2023-300x156.png 300w, https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2022/01/Zhejiang-online-homepage-2023-1024x531.png 1024w, https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2022/01/Zhejiang-online-homepage-2023-768x399.png 768w" sizes="(max-width: 1536px) 100vw, 1536px" /></a><figcaption id="caption-attachment-85176" class="wp-caption-text"><a href="https://www.zjooc.cn/">Zhejiang Provincial MOOC Platform homepage</a> in 2023</figcaption></figure>
<p>The Zhejiang Institutions of Higher Learning Online Open Course Sharing Platform — or <a href="https://www.zjooc.cn/">Zhejiang Provincial MOOC Platform</a> for short — is backed by the Education Department of the province of Zhejiang, south of Shanghai. There are <a href="https://www.zjooc.cn/" target="_blank" rel="noopener">17,500</a> courses offered on the platform.</p>
<h2 id="E-Huixue">E-Huixue</h2>
<figure id="attachment_85177" aria-describedby="caption-attachment-85177" style="width: 1536px" class="wp-caption alignnone"><a href="https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2022/01/e-huixue-homepage-2023.png"><img loading="lazy" class="wp-image-85177 size-full" src="https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2022/01/e-huixue-homepage-2023.png" alt="" width="1536" height="957" srcset="https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2022/01/e-huixue-homepage-2023.png 1536w, https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2022/01/e-huixue-homepage-2023-300x187.png 300w, https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2022/01/e-huixue-homepage-2023-1024x638.png 1024w, https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2022/01/e-huixue-homepage-2023-768x479.png 768w" sizes="(max-width: 1536px) 100vw, 1536px" /></a><figcaption id="caption-attachment-85177" class="wp-caption-text"><a href="http://www.ehuixue.cn/">E-Huixue homepage</a> in 2023</figcaption></figure>
<p>In December 2015, the Department of Education of the Aihui District, situated in the northwest of China, launched <a href="http://www.ehuixue.cn/">E-Huixue</a>. Like Zhejiang’s Provincial MOOC Platform, the purpose of E-Huixue is to serve as a regional repository for online courses. The platform offers more than <a href="https://www.ehuixue.cn/index/clist/index.html" target="_blank" rel="noopener">2500</a> MOOCs with a free digital certificate.</p>
<h2 id="CQOOC">CQOOC</h2>
<figure id="attachment_85178" aria-describedby="caption-attachment-85178" style="width: 1536px" class="wp-caption alignnone"><a href="https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2022/01/cqooc-homepage-2023.png"><img loading="lazy" class="wp-image-85178 size-full" src="https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2022/01/cqooc-homepage-2023.png" alt="" width="1536" height="899" srcset="https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2022/01/cqooc-homepage-2023.png 1536w, https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2022/01/cqooc-homepage-2023-300x176.png 300w, https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2022/01/cqooc-homepage-2023-1024x599.png 1024w, https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2022/01/cqooc-homepage-2023-768x450.png 768w" sizes="(max-width: 1536px) 100vw, 1536px" /></a><figcaption id="caption-attachment-85178" class="wp-caption-text"><a href="http://www.cqooc.com/">CQOOC homepage</a> in 2023</figcaption></figure>
<p><a href="http://www.cqooc.com/">Chongqing University Open Online Learning Platform</a> (CQOOC), was established by the Ministry of Education in <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Chongqing" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Chongqing</a> (a <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Direct-administered_municipalities_of_China" target="_blank" rel="noopener">municipality</a> in southwest China) in June 2016. Around <a href="http://www.cqooc.com/course?el=2" target="_blank" rel="noopener">4300</a> courses, mostly from universities and colleges in Chongqing, are offered on the platform.</p>
<h2 id="Rong-You-Xue-Tang">Rong You Xue Tang</h2>
<figure id="attachment_85179" aria-describedby="caption-attachment-85179" style="width: 1024px" class="wp-caption alignnone"><a href="https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2022/01/rong-homepage-2023.png"><img loading="lazy" class="wp-image-85179 size-full" src="https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2022/01/rong-homepage-2023.png" alt="" width="1024" height="532" srcset="https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2022/01/rong-homepage-2023.png 1024w, https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2022/01/rong-homepage-2023-300x156.png 300w, https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2022/01/rong-homepage-2023-768x399.png 768w" sizes="(max-width: 1024px) 100vw, 1024px" /></a><figcaption id="caption-attachment-85179" class="wp-caption-text"><a href="http://www.livedu.com.cn/ispace4.0/moocMainIndex/mainIndex.do">Rong You Xue Tang homepage</a> in 2023</figcaption></figure>
<p>Rong You Xue Tang is the new name of the former Beijing MOOC Research Association platform. It was founded in 2016 by Renmin University of China together with several Beijing-based universities. Over <a href="http://www.livedu.com.cn/ispace4.0/moocxjkc/queryAllKc.do" target="_blank" rel="noopener">210 free courses</a> are provided on the platform, some of which are <a href="https://www.livedu.com.cn/ispace4.0/moocXwwh/moocqueryXwByid?xwid=AE50F17B26C8EC2FE050007F0100194F" target="_blank" rel="noopener">credit-eligible</a> courses.</p>
<h2 id="Ulearning">Ulearning</h2>
<figure id="attachment_85180" aria-describedby="caption-attachment-85180" style="width: 1536px" class="wp-caption alignnone"><a href="https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2022/01/ulearning-homepage-2023.png"><img loading="lazy" class="wp-image-85180 size-full" src="https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2022/01/ulearning-homepage-2023.png" alt="" width="1536" height="797" srcset="https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2022/01/ulearning-homepage-2023.png 1536w, https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2022/01/ulearning-homepage-2023-300x156.png 300w, https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2022/01/ulearning-homepage-2023-1024x531.png 1024w, https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2022/01/ulearning-homepage-2023-768x399.png 768w" sizes="(max-width: 1536px) 100vw, 1536px" /></a><figcaption id="caption-attachment-85180" class="wp-caption-text"><a href="https://www.ulearning.cn/portal/index.html#/index/portal">Ulearning homepage</a> in 2023</figcaption></figure>
<p><a href="https://www.ulearning.cn/portal/index.html#/index/portal">Ulearning</a> was launched by the online learning company <a href="http://www.ulearning.com.cn/about_profiles.html" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Ulearning</a> in May 2015. There are close to <a href="https://www.ulearning.cn/portal/index.html#/index/openCourse" target="_blank" rel="noopener">2700</a> courses provided on the platform.</p>
<h2 id="ICVE-MOOC-College">ICVE MOOC College</h2>
<figure id="attachment_85181" aria-describedby="caption-attachment-85181" style="width: 1536px" class="wp-caption alignnone"><a href="https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2022/01/ivce-homepage-2023.png"><img loading="lazy" class="wp-image-85181 size-full" src="https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2022/01/ivce-homepage-2023.png" alt="" width="1536" height="982" srcset="https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2022/01/ivce-homepage-2023.png 1536w, https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2022/01/ivce-homepage-2023-300x192.png 300w, https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2022/01/ivce-homepage-2023-1024x655.png 1024w, https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2022/01/ivce-homepage-2023-768x491.png 768w" sizes="(max-width: 1536px) 100vw, 1536px" /></a><figcaption id="caption-attachment-85181" class="wp-caption-text"><a href="https://icve-mooc.icve.com.cn/">ICVE homepage</a> in 2023</figcaption></figure>
<p><a href="https://icve-mooc.icve.com.cn/">ICVE</a> was built for professional education by <a href="http://www.hep.com.cn/" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Higher Education Press</a> in 2014. There are over <a href="https://icve-mooc.icve.com.cn/cms/moocCourse/index.htm">7300</a> free courses offered on the platform, and over 80% of them provide a free certificate.</p>
<h2 id="ICC">ICC</h2>
<figure id="attachment_85182" aria-describedby="caption-attachment-85182" style="width: 1536px" class="wp-caption alignnone"><a href="https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2022/01/icc-homepage-2023.png"><img loading="lazy" class="wp-image-85182 size-full" src="https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2022/01/icc-homepage-2023.png" alt="" width="1536" height="982" srcset="https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2022/01/icc-homepage-2023.png 1536w, https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2022/01/icc-homepage-2023-300x192.png 300w, https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2022/01/icc-homepage-2023-1024x655.png 1024w, https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2022/01/icc-homepage-2023-768x491.png 768w" sizes="(max-width: 1536px) 100vw, 1536px" /></a><figcaption id="caption-attachment-85182" class="wp-caption-text"><a href="http://icc.hep.com.cn/">ICC homepage</a> in 2023</figcaption></figure>
<p><a href="http://icc.hep.com.cn/">ICC</a> was launched by <a href="http://www.hep.com.cn/" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Higher Education Press</a> in 2016. More than <a href="https://icc.hep.com.cn/homeAllCourse.action" target="_blank" rel="noopener">4000</a> courses from <a href="https://icc.hep.com.cn/homeAllSchool.action" target="_blank" rel="noopener">210</a> universities are offered on the platform.</p>
<h2 id="ErYa">ErYa</h2>
<figure id="attachment_85183" aria-describedby="caption-attachment-85183" style="width: 1536px" class="wp-caption alignnone"><a href="https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2022/01/ErYa-homepage-2023.png"><img loading="lazy" class="wp-image-85183 size-full" src="https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2022/01/ErYa-homepage-2023.png" alt="" width="1536" height="805" srcset="https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2022/01/ErYa-homepage-2023.png 1536w, https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2022/01/ErYa-homepage-2023-300x157.png 300w, https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2022/01/ErYa-homepage-2023-1024x537.png 1024w, https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2022/01/ErYa-homepage-2023-768x403.png 768w" sizes="(max-width: 1536px) 100vw, 1536px" /></a><figcaption id="caption-attachment-85183" class="wp-caption-text"><a href="http://erya.mooc.chaoxing.com/">ErYa homepage</a> in 2023</figcaption></figure>
<p><a href="http://erya.mooc.chaoxing.com/">ErYa</a> was launched in January 2015 by the Chaoxing Group, an edtech corporation based in Beijing. The MOOC platform offers around <a href="http://erya.mooc.chaoxing.com/engine2/general/more?t=74115A8FB97F7D0818B962CED639690CD719A9A2BD60988D17620715E89547CEB516A82E93540ECA5645E68AE76744E2">500</a> free courses in liberal arts from humanities to creative thinking.</p>
<h2 id="gaoxiaobang">Gaoxiaobang</h2>
<figure id="attachment_85184" aria-describedby="caption-attachment-85184" style="width: 1536px" class="wp-caption alignnone"><a href="https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2022/01/gaoxiaobang-homepage-2023.png"><img loading="lazy" class="wp-image-85184 size-full" src="https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2022/01/gaoxiaobang-homepage-2023.png" alt="" width="1536" height="766" srcset="https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2022/01/gaoxiaobang-homepage-2023.png 1536w, https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2022/01/gaoxiaobang-homepage-2023-300x150.png 300w, https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2022/01/gaoxiaobang-homepage-2023-1024x511.png 1024w, https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2022/01/gaoxiaobang-homepage-2023-768x383.png 768w" sizes="(max-width: 1536px) 100vw, 1536px" /></a><figcaption id="caption-attachment-85184" class="wp-caption-text"><a href="https://imooc.gaoxiaobang.com/">Gaoxiaobang homepage</a> in 2023</figcaption></figure>
<p><a href="https://imooc.gaoxiaobang.com/">Gaoxiaobang</a> was established by a subsidiary of <a href="https://www.huike.com/index" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Huike Group</a>, a company focused on the upskilling and reskilling of professionals in tech-related domains. The platform was launched in September 2015, and it currently offers close to <a href="https://imooc.gaoxiaobang.com/#/courses" target="_blank" rel="noopener">470</a> free courses.</p>
<h2 id="PMPHMOOC">PMPHMOOC</h2>
<figure id="attachment_85185" aria-describedby="caption-attachment-85185" style="width: 1024px" class="wp-caption alignnone"><a href="https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2022/01/PMPHMOOC-homepage-2023.png"><img loading="lazy" class="wp-image-85185 size-full" src="https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2022/01/PMPHMOOC-homepage-2023.png" alt="" width="1024" height="528" srcset="https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2022/01/PMPHMOOC-homepage-2023.png 1024w, https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2022/01/PMPHMOOC-homepage-2023-300x155.png 300w, https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2022/01/PMPHMOOC-homepage-2023-768x396.png 768w" sizes="(max-width: 1024px) 100vw, 1024px" /></a><figcaption id="caption-attachment-85185" class="wp-caption-text"><a href="http://www.pmphmooc.com/">PMPHMOOC homepage</a> in 2023</figcaption></figure>
<p><a href="http://www.pmphmooc.com/">PMPHMOOC</a> was established in 2015 by the medical publisher <a href="https://www.pmph.com/" target="_blank" rel="noopener">People’s Medical Publishing House</a> in partnership with medical schools and academic institutions across China. It provides <a href="http://www.pmphmooc.com/mooc_system/#/moocIndex">70 health-related MOOCs</a> in 10 subjects — for instance, in anatomy and biochemistry.</p>
<h2 id="UMOOCs">UMOOCs</h2>
<figure id="attachment_85186" aria-describedby="caption-attachment-85186" style="width: 1536px" class="wp-caption alignnone"><a href="https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2022/01/umoocs-homepage-2023.png"><img loading="lazy" class="wp-image-85186 size-full" src="https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2022/01/umoocs-homepage-2023.png" alt="" width="1536" height="733" srcset="https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2022/01/umoocs-homepage-2023.png 1536w, https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2022/01/umoocs-homepage-2023-300x143.png 300w, https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2022/01/umoocs-homepage-2023-1024x489.png 1024w, https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2022/01/umoocs-homepage-2023-768x367.png 768w" sizes="(max-width: 1536px) 100vw, 1536px" /></a><figcaption id="caption-attachment-85186" class="wp-caption-text"><a href="http://moocs.unipus.cn/">UMOOCs homepage</a> in 2023</figcaption></figure>
<p><a href="http://moocs.unipus.cn/">UMOOCs</a> is a Chinese MOOC platform for studying foreign languages. The platform was founded by Beijing Foreign Studies University in December 2017, and it is affiliated with the Foreign Language Teaching and Research Press, a publishing company dedicated to all facets of foreign language study in China. It offers over <a href="http://moocs.unipus.cn/course/explore" target="_blank" rel="noopener">400 free courses with certificate</a> covering 10 languages.</p>
<h2 id="iLab-X">iLab-X</h2>
<figure id="attachment_85187" aria-describedby="caption-attachment-85187" style="width: 1536px" class="wp-caption alignnone"><a href="https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2022/01/ilabx-homepage-2023.png"><img loading="lazy" class="wp-image-85187 size-full" src="https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2022/01/ilabx-homepage-2023.png" alt="" width="1536" height="772" srcset="https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2022/01/ilabx-homepage-2023.png 1536w, https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2022/01/ilabx-homepage-2023-300x151.png 300w, https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2022/01/ilabx-homepage-2023-1024x515.png 1024w, https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2022/01/ilabx-homepage-2023-768x386.png 768w" sizes="(max-width: 1536px) 100vw, 1536px" /></a><figcaption id="caption-attachment-85187" class="wp-caption-text"><a href="http://www.ilab-x.com/">iLab-X homepage</a> in 2023</figcaption></figure>
<p><a href="http://www.ilab-x.com/">iLab-X</a> is a MOOC platform for virtual simulation experiments launched by <a href="http://www.hep.com.cn/" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Higher Education Press</a> in 2017. Close to <a href="http://www.ilab-x.com/list" target="_blank" rel="noopener">3500</a> virtual experiments are provided on the platform.</p>
<h2 id="MOEC">MOEC</h2>
<figure id="attachment_85188" aria-describedby="caption-attachment-85188" style="width: 1537px" class="wp-caption alignnone"><a href="https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2022/01/moec-homepage-2023.png"><img loading="lazy" class="wp-image-85188 size-full" src="https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2022/01/moec-homepage-2023.png" alt="" width="1537" height="964" srcset="https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2022/01/moec-homepage-2023.png 1537w, https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2022/01/moec-homepage-2023-300x188.png 300w, https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2022/01/moec-homepage-2023-1024x642.png 1024w, https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2022/01/moec-homepage-2023-768x482.png 768w" sizes="(max-width: 1537px) 100vw, 1537px" /></a><figcaption id="caption-attachment-85188" class="wp-caption-text"><a href="https://yxsypt.com/training/manage/portal/">MOEC homepage</a> in 2023</figcaption></figure>
<p><a href="https://yxsypt.com/training/manage/portal/">MOEC</a> is a MOOC platform for virtual simulation experiment education in medicine, launched by the company <a href="http://www.mengoo.com/" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Mengoo</a> in 2020. The MOOC platform has provided around <a href="https://yxsypt.com/training/manage/portal/curriculum.html" target="_blank" rel="noopener">720</a> courses in medicine for over <a href="https://yxsypt.com/training/manage/portal/cooperativeUniversity.html" target="_blank" rel="noopener">100</a> university medical schools in China.</p>
<h2 id="Educoder">Educoder</h2>
<figure id="attachment_85189" aria-describedby="caption-attachment-85189" style="width: 1537px" class="wp-caption alignnone"><a href="https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2022/01/educoder-homepage-2023.png"><img loading="lazy" class="wp-image-85189 size-full" src="https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2022/01/educoder-homepage-2023.png" alt="" width="1537" height="641" srcset="https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2022/01/educoder-homepage-2023.png 1537w, https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2022/01/educoder-homepage-2023-300x125.png 300w, https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2022/01/educoder-homepage-2023-1024x427.png 1024w, https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2022/01/educoder-homepage-2023-768x320.png 768w" sizes="(max-width: 1537px) 100vw, 1537px" /></a><figcaption id="caption-attachment-85189" class="wp-caption-text"><a href="https://www.educoder.net/">MOEC homepage</a> in 2023</figcaption></figure>
<p><a href="https://www.educoder.net/">Educoder</a> is a MOOC platform for computer science and programming that was launched in July 2016. There are over <a href="https://www.educoder.net/paths" target="_blank" rel="noopener">640</a> free courses and thousands of free programming exercises. The MOOC platform also allows its verified users to create their own courses, exercises, and <a href="https://www.educoder.net/classrooms" target="_blank" rel="noopener">online classrooms</a>.</p>
<h2 id="eWant">eWant</h2>
<figure id="attachment_85190" aria-describedby="caption-attachment-85190" style="width: 1537px" class="wp-caption alignnone"><a href="https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2022/01/ewant-homepage-2023.png"><img loading="lazy" class="wp-image-85190 size-full" src="https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2022/01/ewant-homepage-2023.png" alt="" width="1537" height="644" srcset="https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2022/01/ewant-homepage-2023.png 1537w, https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2022/01/ewant-homepage-2023-300x126.png 300w, https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2022/01/ewant-homepage-2023-1024x429.png 1024w, https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2022/01/ewant-homepage-2023-768x322.png 768w" sizes="(max-width: 1537px) 100vw, 1537px" /></a><figcaption id="caption-attachment-85190" class="wp-caption-text"><a href="http://www.ewant.org/">eWant homepage</a> in 2023</figcaption></figure>
<p><a href="http://www.ewant.org/">eWant</a> is a MOOC platform that was launched by National Chiao Tung University in 2013. National Chiao Tung University is one of Taiwan’s leading public research universities, located in Hsinchu, Taiwan. It hosts more than <a href="https://www.ewant.org/admin/tool/mooccourse/allcourses.php" target="_blank" rel="noopener">3200</a> courses from over <a href="https://www.ewant.org/local/school/list.php?lang=en" target="_blank" rel="noopener">90</a> different universities.</p>

<figure id="attachment_85191" aria-describedby="caption-attachment-85191" style="width: 1537px" class="wp-caption alignnone"><a href="https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2022/01/sharecourse-homepage-2023.png"><img loading="lazy" class="wp-image-85191 size-full" src="https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2022/01/sharecourse-homepage-2023.png" alt="" width="1537" height="859" srcset="https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2022/01/sharecourse-homepage-2023.png 1537w, https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2022/01/sharecourse-homepage-2023-300x168.png 300w, https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2022/01/sharecourse-homepage-2023-1024x572.png 1024w, https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2022/01/sharecourse-homepage-2023-768x429.png 768w" sizes="(max-width: 1537px) 100vw, 1537px" /></a><figcaption id="caption-attachment-85191" class="wp-caption-text"><a href="https://www.sharecourse.net/">ShareCourse homepage</a> in 2023</figcaption></figure>

About <a href="https://www.sharecourse.net/sharecourse/course/view/categorySearch/6/23?type=2" target="_blank" rel="noopener">190</a> of them are free.</p>

		<title>Futurism and Space Exploration: a Perfect Start to the Wilder Side of Space Research</title>
		<link>https://www.classcentral.com/report/review-futurism-and-space-exploration/</link>
					<comments>https://www.classcentral.com/report/review-futurism-and-space-exploration/#respond</comments>
		
		<dc:creator><![CDATA[Kendahl Edwards]]></dc:creator>
		<pubDate>Thu, 02 Feb 2023 15:25:41 +0000</pubDate>
				<category><![CDATA[Reviews]]></category>
		<guid isPermaLink="false">https://www.classcentral.com/report/?p=85148</guid>

					<description><![CDATA[<p>This is an in-depth review of the Futurism and Space Exploration series by PBS Space Time.</p>
<p>The post <a rel="nofollow" href="https://www.classcentral.com/report/review-futurism-and-space-exploration/">Futurism and Space Exploration: a Perfect Start to the Wilder Side of Space Research</a> appeared first on <a rel="nofollow" href="https://www.classcentral.com/report">The Report by Class Central</a>.</p>
]]></description>
										<content:encoded><![CDATA[<figure id="attachment_85149" aria-describedby="caption-attachment-85149" style="width: 1024px" class="wp-caption alignnone"><img loading="lazy" class="wp-image-85149 size-full" src="https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2023/02/Futurism-and-Space-Exploration-Should-We-Colonize-Venus-Instead-of-Mars_.png" alt="" width="1024" height="512" srcset="https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2023/02/Futurism-and-Space-Exploration-Should-We-Colonize-Venus-Instead-of-Mars_.png 1024w, https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2023/02/Futurism-and-Space-Exploration-Should-We-Colonize-Venus-Instead-of-Mars_-300x150.png 300w, https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2023/02/Futurism-and-Space-Exploration-Should-We-Colonize-Venus-Instead-of-Mars_-768x384.png 768w" sizes="(max-width: 1024px) 100vw, 1024px" /><figcaption id="caption-attachment-85149" class="wp-caption-text">Dr. Gabe Perez-Giz, course instructor. From &#8220;Should We Colonize Venus Instead of Mars?&#8221;</figcaption></figure>
<p>Has the vastness of space ever made your head spin at the speed of light? Have you ever wondered what a Dyson sphere is? Maybe you have a few questions about what people born on Mars would look like. In this course all these questions will be answered and so will many more. <a href="https://www.classcentral.com/course/youtube-futurism-and-space-exploration-53137" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Futurism and Space Exploration</a> is a fun and self-paced way to learn the answers to questions the amateur stargazer and space lover may have. The best part is that it’s all in bite-sized videos that are easy to binge.</p>
<h2>Who should take this course?</h2>
<p>Anyone with a love for space and a few out of the box questions about the more odd and interesting parts of space. If you are a beginner in star gazing and a person who yearns for straightforward easy to understand answers to unexpected questions, this course is for you. I would suggest it to students who would like a space themed hobby or those looking for a pastime that remains interesting even after the course as the answer given can be expanded on and discussed even further on other forums.</p>
<h2>The instructors</h2>
<figure id="attachment_85151" aria-describedby="caption-attachment-85151" style="width: 1024px" class="wp-caption alignnone"><img loading="lazy" class="size-full wp-image-85151" src="https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2023/02/Futurism-and-Space-Exploration-Are-We-Alone_-Galactic-Civilization-Challenge.png" alt="" width="1024" height="512" srcset="https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2023/02/Futurism-and-Space-Exploration-Are-We-Alone_-Galactic-Civilization-Challenge.png 1024w, https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2023/02/Futurism-and-Space-Exploration-Are-We-Alone_-Galactic-Civilization-Challenge-300x150.png 300w, https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2023/02/Futurism-and-Space-Exploration-Are-We-Alone_-Galactic-Civilization-Challenge-768x384.png 768w" sizes="(max-width: 1024px) 100vw, 1024px" /><figcaption id="caption-attachment-85151" class="wp-caption-text">Dr. Matt O’Dowd, course instructor. From &#8220;Are We Alone? Galactic Civilization Challenge&#8221;.</figcaption></figure>
<p>The course is presented by PBS Space Time through YouTube and hosted by the quick paced smooth-talking physicist Dr. Gabe Perez-Giz and mellow-minded super-intellectual astrophysicist Dr. Matt O’Dowd. The two writers of the series gave easy to understand and logical answers in such as to simulate a casual discussion which helped in understanding the concepts presented in the series.</p>
<h2>What will you learn?</h2>
<p>We’ll not spoil all the surprises, but here’s a rough overview of what is covered in the course:</p>
<ul>
<li>        Exoplanets and where they are found.</li>
<li>        Dyson spheres- what are they and how would we make one?</li>
<li>        Terraforming planets and what we need to survive on another planet.</li>
<li>        What secret NASA projects have been used in our daily lives.</li>
<li>        How do wormholes work?</li>
<li>        Can we reach hyper speed or travel at the speed of light?</li>
<li>        The potential asteroid mining revolution.</li>
</ul>
<figure id="attachment_85152" aria-describedby="caption-attachment-85152" style="width: 1024px" class="wp-caption alignnone"><img loading="lazy" class="size-full wp-image-85152" src="https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2023/02/Futurism-and-Space-Exploration-How-Asteroid-Mining-Will-Save-Earth.png" alt="" width="1024" height="512" srcset="https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2023/02/Futurism-and-Space-Exploration-How-Asteroid-Mining-Will-Save-Earth.png 1024w, https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2023/02/Futurism-and-Space-Exploration-How-Asteroid-Mining-Will-Save-Earth-300x150.png 300w, https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2023/02/Futurism-and-Space-Exploration-How-Asteroid-Mining-Will-Save-Earth-768x384.png 768w" sizes="(max-width: 1024px) 100vw, 1024px" /><figcaption id="caption-attachment-85152" class="wp-caption-text">From &#8220;How Asteroid Mining Will Save Earth&#8221;.</figcaption></figure>
<p>To give you more information would ruin the fun of taking the course. The only way to find out all the questions and their respective answers is to watch the entire series.</p>
<h2>Requirements</h2>
<p>No degrees or formal education on the topics discussed is required. I would suggest a prior exposure to a few very basic principles of space is needed to fully grasp the gravity of the concepts discussed. The course is only about 4-hours long and is completely self-paced which allows you to take as much time as you need. I suggest a video a day which is about 10-15 minutes. This gives you about 20 days of interesting concepts and topics to ponder over.</p>
<h2>Personal experience</h2>
<figure id="attachment_85150" aria-describedby="caption-attachment-85150" style="width: 1024px" class="wp-caption alignnone"><img loading="lazy" class="size-full wp-image-85150" src="https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2023/02/Futurism-and-Space-Exploration-What-Will-Destroy-Planet-Earth_.png" alt="" width="1024" height="512" srcset="https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2023/02/Futurism-and-Space-Exploration-What-Will-Destroy-Planet-Earth_.png 1024w, https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2023/02/Futurism-and-Space-Exploration-What-Will-Destroy-Planet-Earth_-300x150.png 300w, https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2023/02/Futurism-and-Space-Exploration-What-Will-Destroy-Planet-Earth_-768x384.png 768w" sizes="(max-width: 1024px) 100vw, 1024px" /><figcaption id="caption-attachment-85150" class="wp-caption-text">From &#8220;What Will Destroy Planet Earth?&#8221;</figcaption></figure>
<p>I personally enjoyed the entire series. The short video format kept me engaged long enough to truly have a good understanding of the lesson and remained short enough to not bore me. The course is made for people with short attention spans and short bursts of time throughout their day. I felt like I learnt quite a lot without being bombarded with information or being left confused at the end of a lesson. The topics to this day remain relevant and interesting. The various lessons inspired me to look deeper into space and futurism.</p>
<p>In conclusion, the course is well scripted and written in such a way to keep the viewer engaged. The topics remained relevant and the short form is very digestible for those with odd working hours or short periods of free time. The hosts and writers are very knowledgeable and truly have a good way of explaining complex terminology. A brilliant course that anyone with a love for space should watch.</p>
<p>A course that is similar in style and topic is <a href="https://www.classcentral.com/course/youtube-the-universe-and-space-stuff-47958" target="_blank" rel="noopener">The Universe and Space stuff by Kurzgesagt- In a Nutshell</a>.</p>

<h2><span style="font-weight: 400;">What is American Sign Language (ASL)?</span></h2>
<p><span style="font-weight: 400;">American Sign Language (ASL) is a natural language and is the primary language of the deaf community in the United States of America and in many parts of Canada. It is a visual language expressed by hand movements, facial expressions and body posture.</span></p>
<p><span style="font-weight: 400;">Sign language is not universal – different sign languages are used in different countries and regions. Some countries also adopt features of ASL in their sign languages. Like any spoken language, ASL has its own grammar and syntax that differs from English – its own rules for pronunciation, word formation and word order.</span></p>
<h3><span style="font-weight: 400;">Why are American Sign Language (ASL) Skills Important?</span></h3>
<p><span style="font-weight: 400;">In the USA, there are about 48 million people with hearing impairment, from which an estimate of </span><a href="https://www.accessibility.com/blog/do-all-deaf-people-use-sign-language" target="_blank" rel="noopener"><span style="font-weight: 400;">500,000 can sign language</span></a><span style="font-weight: 400;">. Considering that service providers, educators, friends and relatives will also have some level of expertise, this number can be even higher.</span></p>
<p><span style="font-weight: 400;">Learning any language is not just about memorizing hundreds or thousands of words – you can also participate in a new community of people and better understand the </span><a href="https://deafculturecentre.ca/what-is-deaf-culture/" target="_blank" rel="noopener"><span style="font-weight: 400;">Deaf Culture</span></a><span style="font-weight: 400;">. Anyone can </span><a href="https://www.healthyhearing.com/report/52606-Why-you-should-learn-sign-language-in-the-new-year" target="_blank" rel="noopener"><span style="font-weight: 400;">benefit from being able to communicate with the deaf and hard of hearing</span></a><span style="font-weight: 400;">, parents, educators, first responders, and service providers, just to name a few.</span></p>
<p><span style="font-weight: 400;">And if you want to make a career out of it, there are thousands of jobs for Sign Language Interpreters on </span><a href="https://www.indeed.com/jobs?q=Sign+Language+Interpreter&amp;l=United+States&amp;vjk=e5848a5600cbfcbd" target="_blank" rel="noopener"><span style="font-weight: 400;">Indeed</span></a><span style="font-weight: 400;">, </span><a href="https://www.linkedin.com/jobs/sign-language-interpreter-jobs/?currentJobId=3434891872" target="_blank" rel="noopener"><span style="font-weight: 400;">LinkedIn</span></a><span style="font-weight: 400;">, and </span><a href="https://www.glassdoor.com/Job/asl-interpreter-jobs-SRCH_KO0,15.htm" target="_blank" rel="noopener"><span style="font-weight: 400;">Glassdoor</span></a><span style="font-weight: 400;"> with an average salary of </span><a href="https://www.indeed.com/career/sign-language-interpreter/salaries" target="_blank" rel="noopener"><span style="font-weight: 400;">$29 per hour</span></a><span style="font-weight: 400;">.</span></p>
<h3><span style="font-weight: 400;">What is My Experience with American Sign Language (ASL)?</span></h3>
<p><span style="font-weight: 400;">I am a </span><a href="https://www.coursera.org/instructor/archisha-bhar" target="_blank" rel="noopener"><span style="font-weight: 400;">Guided Project Instructor</span></a><span style="font-weight: 400;"> and a Beta Tester at Coursera, having tested many courses before they’re officially launched. I have taken </span><a href="https://www.classcentral.com/@archisha" target="_blank" rel="noopener"><span style="font-weight: 400;">over 50 online courses</span></a><span style="font-weight: 400;"> in various subjects.</span></p>
<p><span style="font-weight: 400;">My experience as an online learner and teacher has given me some perspective on what to look for in an online course. I used my experience to evaluate each course in this list.</span></p>
<p><a href="https://www.classcentral.com/" target="_blank" rel="noopener"><img loading="lazy" class="alignnone wp-image-79247 size-full" src="https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2022/03/Class-Central-Preview-1.png" alt="Find your next course." width="1024" height="512" srcset="https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2022/03/Class-Central-Preview-1.png 1024w, https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2022/03/Class-Central-Preview-1-300x150.png 300w, https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2022/03/Class-Central-Preview-1-768x384.png 768w" sizes="(max-width: 1024px) 100vw, 1024px" /></a></p>
<h2><span style="font-weight: 400;">Course Ranking Methodology</span></h2>
<p><span style="font-weight: 400;">I built this ranking following the now tried-and-tested methodology I used in previous rankings (</span><a href="https://www.classcentral.com/report/category/best-courses/" target="_blank" rel="noopener"><span style="font-weight: 400;">you can find them all here</span></a><span style="font-weight: 400;">). It involves a three-step process:</span></p>
<ol>
<li style="font-weight: 400;" aria-level="1"><b>Research:</b><span style="font-weight: 400;"> I started by leveraging Class Central’s database with </span><a href="https://www.classcentral.com/subjects" target="_blank" rel="noopener"><span style="font-weight: 400;">100K online courses</span></a><span style="font-weight: 400;"> and 200K+ reviews. Then, I made a preliminary selection of </span><a href="https://www.classcentral.com/subject/sign-language" target="_blank" rel="noopener"><span style="font-weight: 400;">50+ Sign Language courses</span></a><span style="font-weight: 400;"> by rating, reviews, and bookmarks.</span></li>
<li style="font-weight: 400;" aria-level="1"><b>Evaluate:</b><span style="font-weight: 400;"> I read through reviews on Class Central, Reddit, and course providers to understand what other learners thought about each course and combined it with my own experience as a </span><a href="https://www.classcentral.com/@archisha" target="_blank" rel="noopener"><span style="font-weight: 400;">learner</span></a><span style="font-weight: 400;">.</span></li>
<li style="font-weight: 400;" aria-level="1"><b>Select:</b><span style="font-weight: 400;"> Well-made courses were picked if they presented valuable and engaging content and they have to fit in a set of criteria and be ranked accordingly: comprehensive curriculum, release date, affordability, ratings and enrollments.</span></li>
</ol>
<p><span style="font-weight: 400;">The end result is a unique selection of courses that combines a decade of Class Central data and my own experience as an online learner to try to get the best of both worlds. So far, I’ve spent more than 10 hours building this list, and I’ll continue to update it.</span></p>

<h2 id="anchor-1"><span style="font-weight: 400;">1. </span><a href="https://www.classcentral.com/course/independent-asl-university-lessons-121047" target="_blank" rel="noopener"><span style="font-weight: 400;">ASL University: Lessons (ASL University)</span></a></h2>
<figure id="attachment_85088" aria-describedby="caption-attachment-85088" style="width: 1537px" class="wp-caption alignnone"><img loading="lazy" class="size-full wp-image-85088" src="https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2023/01/1.-ASL-University_-Lessons-ASL-University.png" alt="" width="1537" height="769" srcset="https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2023/01/1.-ASL-University_-Lessons-ASL-University.png 1537w, https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2023/01/1.-ASL-University_-Lessons-ASL-University-300x150.png 300w, https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2023/01/1.-ASL-University_-Lessons-ASL-University-1024x512.png 1024w, https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2023/01/1.-ASL-University_-Lessons-ASL-University-768x384.png 768w" sizes="(max-width: 1537px) 100vw, 1537px" /><figcaption id="caption-attachment-85088" class="wp-caption-text">Bill Vicars (left), instructor</figcaption></figure>
<p><span style="font-weight: 400;">My first pick for the best American Sign Language (ASL) online course is the </span><b>free course</b> <a href="https://www.classcentral.com/course/independent-asl-university-lessons-121047" target="_blank" rel="noopener"><i><span style="font-weight: 400;">ASL University: Lessons</span></i></a><span style="font-weight: 400;">, offered by ASL University.</span></p>
<p><span style="font-weight: 400;">In this comprehensive course with hundreds of hours of engaging video lectures, interactive quizzes, and plenty of learning resources you’ll learn from scratch how to be a great communicator in sign language with the specialist Dr. William Vicars.</span></p>
<p><span style="font-weight: 400;">Vicars will build your confidence from the ground up, starting from spelling and simple daily sentences to more and more abstract concepts. He uses evidence based language learning with reinforcement, repetition, and a curriculum that covers the most frequent vocabulary from lesson one. </span></p>
<p><span style="font-weight: 400;">Every lesson is given with an accompanying learner that will give you the opportunity to feel like you’re in a private class with the instructor and surely you won’t get bored while learning.</span></p>
<h3><span style="font-weight: 400;">What You’ll Learn</span></h3>
<p><span style="font-weight: 400;">In this course, you’ll cover 46 themed-based lessons:</span></p>
<p><span style="font-weight: 400;">In the first 30 lessons, you&#8217;ll learn the basics you need to communicate in ASL about yourself, your family, feelings, basic actions, food, clothes, animals, school and work, and traveling.</span></p>
<p><span style="font-weight: 400;">From lesson 31 to 45, you’ll learn more intermediate skills and start learning about more nuances in sign language to talk about more abstract concepts such as emotions and dreams. You’ll learn about sports, giving your opinion, gossip, hand tools, giving directions, holidays, and talking about your health.</span></p>
<p><span style="font-weight: 400;">Finally, you’ll learn more upper-intermediate and advanced concepts in the last 15 lessons: talking about numbers and money, travel, buying things/grocery, reading preferences, dating and relationships, academic, medicine and hospital talk, cars and driving, playing games, goodbyes, and social media.</span></p>
<h3><span style="font-weight: 400;">How You’ll Learn</span></h3>
<p><span style="font-weight: 400;">The course is broken down into 4 modules and 46 lessons. Each module involves about 23 hours of work. Concepts are taught through a combination of videos, readings and quizzes.</span></p>

<p><span style="font-weight: 400;">My second pick for the best American Sign Language (ASL) online course is the </span><b>free course</b> <a href="https://www.classcentral.com/course/youtube-beginner-american-sign-language-asl-course-64482" target="_blank" rel="noopener"><i><span style="font-weight: 400;">Beginner American Sign Language (ASL ) Course</span></i></a><span style="font-weight: 400;">, offered by Laura Berg Life on YouTube.</span></p>
<p><span style="font-weight: 400;">This </span><b>free</b><span style="font-weight: 400;"> course has a good balance of lessons and practice. It starts with basic vocabulary and simple sentences, and gradually moves up to more complex sentences as you learn more ASL signs. At the end of each lesson, there’s a video dedicated to quizzes to test your receptive skills. By the end of the course, you should be able to sign basic ASL words and form simple sentences.</span></p>

<h2 id="anchor-3"><span style="font-weight: 400;">3. </span><a href="https://www.classcentral.com/course/youtube-asl-basics-64490" target="_blank" rel="noopener"><span style="font-weight: 400;">ASL Basics (Learn How to Sign)</span></a></h2>
<figure id="attachment_85090" aria-describedby="caption-attachment-85090" style="width: 1537px" class="wp-caption alignnone"><img loading="lazy" class="size-full wp-image-85090" src="https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2023/01/3.-ASL-Basics-Learn-How-to-Sign.png" alt="" width="1537" height="769" srcset="https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2023/01/3.-ASL-Basics-Learn-How-to-Sign.png 1537w, https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2023/01/3.-ASL-Basics-Learn-How-to-Sign-300x150.png 300w, https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2023/01/3.-ASL-Basics-Learn-How-to-Sign-1024x512.png 1024w, https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2023/01/3.-ASL-Basics-Learn-How-to-Sign-768x384.png 768w" sizes="(max-width: 1537px) 100vw, 1537px" /><figcaption id="caption-attachment-85090" class="wp-caption-text">Meredith, instructor</figcaption></figure>
<p><span style="font-weight: 400;">My third pick for the best American Sign Language (ASL) online course is the </span><b>free course</b> <a href="https://www.classcentral.com/course/youtube-asl-basics-64490" target="_blank" rel="noopener"><i><span style="font-weight: 400;">ASL Basics</span></i></a><span style="font-weight: 400;">, offered by Learn How to Sign on YouTube.</span></p>
<p><span style="font-weight: 400;">Aimed towards beginners, this </span><b>free</b><span style="font-weight: 400;"> ASL course is more of a collection or series of tutorials that teach you how to sign basic ASL words and phrases. The lessons will be helpful in your daily ASL conversations, starting with the alphabet and getting into simple words, common phrases,  greetings, feelings, situation-based signs, ASL sentence structure, and many more.</span></p>
<h3><span style="font-weight: 400;">What You’ll Learn</span></h3>
<p><span style="font-weight: 400;">In this course, you’ll understand the alphabet (ABCs), common and descriptive signs, numbers, questions, animal signs, greetings, farewells and introductions, days of the week and months of the year, affirmation and negation signs, and places around the town.</span></p>
<p><span style="font-weight: 400;">You’ll also learn about describing people, feelings and emotions, barista signs, meat and dairy signs, fruit and veggie signs, food signs, common phrases, summer signs, school signs, money, routines, sentence structure, and profession signs.</span></p>
<h3><span style="font-weight: 400;">How You’ll Learn</span></h3>
<p><span style="font-weight: 400;">The course is broken down into 48 videos. Each video involves about 5 to 10 minutes of work. Concepts are taught through video lectures only.</span></p>

<p><span style="font-weight: 400;">My fourth pick for the best American Sign Language (ASL) online course is </span><a href="https://www.classcentral.com/course/udemy-learnandmastersignlanguage-41287" target="_blank" rel="noopener"><i><span style="font-weight: 400;">Learn &amp; Master Sign Language</span></i></a><span style="font-weight: 400;"> on Udemy.</span></p>
<p><span style="font-weight: 400;">One of the most comprehensive courses on this list, this course for beginners will help you master the receptive and the expressive components of ASL. The lessons are interactive, giving you a solid foundation in basic and advanced signing including vocabulary, sentences, narratives and dialogues. The course also contains enough practice opportunities as well.</span></p>
<h3><span style="font-weight: 400;">What You’ll Learn</span></h3>
<p><span style="font-weight: 400;">You’ll start with the basics which includes introductions, gesturing, the alphabet members of the family, and more. Then, you’ll progress to advanced techniques such as expansion features, classifiers, storytelling, and more. Other topics include how to communicate during emergencies, everyday activities, facts about the dynamic deaf culture, interacting at sporting events, and more.</span></p>
<h3><span style="font-weight: 400;">How You’ll Learn</span></h3>
<p><span style="font-weight: 400;">The course is broken down into 28 sections. Each section involves about 1.5 to 2 hours of work. Concepts are taught through a combination of videos, a lesson book and in-video practice quizzes.</span></p>

<figure id="attachment_85093" aria-describedby="caption-attachment-85093" style="width: 1537px" class="wp-caption alignnone"><img loading="lazy" class="size-full wp-image-85093" src="https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2023/01/6.-ASL-_-Pronouns-Vocab-Practice-_-American-Sign-Language-Skillshare.png" alt="" width="1537" height="769" srcset="https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2023/01/6.-ASL-_-Pronouns-Vocab-Practice-_-American-Sign-Language-Skillshare.png 1537w, https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2023/01/6.-ASL-_-Pronouns-Vocab-Practice-_-American-Sign-Language-Skillshare-300x150.png 300w, https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2023/01/6.-ASL-_-Pronouns-Vocab-Practice-_-American-Sign-Language-Skillshare-1024x512.png 1024w, https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2023/01/6.-ASL-_-Pronouns-Vocab-Practice-_-American-Sign-Language-Skillshare-768x384.png 768w" sizes="(max-width: 1537px) 100vw, 1537px" /><figcaption id="caption-attachment-85093" class="wp-caption-text">Michael, instructor</figcaption></figure>
<p><span style="font-weight: 400;">My sixth pick for the best American Sign Language (ASL) online course is </span><a href="https://www.classcentral.com/course/skillshare-asl-pronouns-vocab-practice-american-sign-language-52670" target="_blank" rel="noopener"><i><span style="font-weight: 400;">ASL | Pronouns + Vocab + Practice | American Sign Language</span></i></a><span style="font-weight: 400;"> on Skillshare.</span></p>
<p><span style="font-weight: 400;">This course focuses specifically on the use of two types of pronouns – personal and possessive  – in ASL. You’ll learn to sign and recognize pronouns in ASL, increase your vocabulary and combine them to create useful phrases and sentences. And you’ll be able to achieve all this within a matter of a couple of hours.</span></p>
<h3><span style="font-weight: 400;">What You’ll Learn</span></h3>
<p><span style="font-weight: 400;">In this course, you’ll learn about handshapes, I/me vs. my/mine, you vs. your, he/she/it vs. his/her/its, pronouns 1st group, we/us vs. our, they/them vs. their, you (plural) vs. your (plural), pronouns 2nd group, and all pronouns.</span></p>
<p><span style="font-weight: 400;">You’ll also explore signs for apple, house, mom, cat, purse and shoes, noun vocabulary signs, pronoun + noun phrases, pronoun + noun (silent), signs for happy, sad, mad, scared, surprised and hungry, pronoun + adjective, and simple sentences (silent).</span></p>
<h3><span style="font-weight: 400;">How You’ll Learn</span></h3>
<p><span style="font-weight: 400;">The course is broken down into 40 lessons. Each lesson involves about 2 to 8 minutes of work. Concepts are taught through a combination of videos and a final assignment.</span></p>

<h2 id="anchor-10"><span style="font-weight: 400;">10. </span><a href="https://www.classcentral.com/course/youtube-starter-signs-baby-sign-language-64511" target="_blank" rel="noopener"><span style="font-weight: 400;">Starter Signs &#8211; Baby Sign Language (TalkBoxMom)</span></a></h2>
<figure id="attachment_85096" aria-describedby="caption-attachment-85096" style="width: 1537px" class="wp-caption alignnone"><img loading="lazy" class="size-full wp-image-85096" src="https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2023/01/10.-Starter-Signs-Baby-Sign-Language-TalkBoxMom.png" alt="" width="1537" height="769" srcset="https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2023/01/10.-Starter-Signs-Baby-Sign-Language-TalkBoxMom.png 1537w, https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2023/01/10.-Starter-Signs-Baby-Sign-Language-TalkBoxMom-300x150.png 300w, https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2023/01/10.-Starter-Signs-Baby-Sign-Language-TalkBoxMom-1024x512.png 1024w, https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2023/01/10.-Starter-Signs-Baby-Sign-Language-TalkBoxMom-768x384.png 768w" sizes="(max-width: 1537px) 100vw, 1537px" /><figcaption id="caption-attachment-85096" class="wp-caption-text">Adelaide Olguin, instructor</figcaption></figure>
<p><span style="font-weight: 400;">My tenth pick for the best American Sign Language (ASL) online course is the </span><b>free course</b> <a href="https://www.classcentral.com/course/youtube-starter-signs-baby-sign-language-64511" target="_blank" rel="noopener"><i><span style="font-weight: 400;">Starter Signs &#8211; Baby Sign Language</span></i></a><span style="font-weight: 400;">, offered by TalkBoxMom on YouTube.</span></p>
<p><span style="font-weight: 400;">Babies pick up sign language fast. So it’s best to start teaching early. This short </span><b>free</b><span style="font-weight: 400;"> course is specially made for babies (well actually their parents of course!) so that they can teach their babies simple words and phrases in ASL.</span></p>
<h3><span style="font-weight: 400;">What You’ll Learn</span></h3>
<p><span style="font-weight: 400;">In this course, you’ll learn different words and phrases in baby sign language such as finished, again, pretty, blanket, binky, banana, stop, beautiful, book, all done, change diaper, clean up, cold, cook, cup, cracker, come, want, like, doll, dance, dad, dirty, close, french fries, fall off, down, drink, eat, fall down, and fan.</span></p>
<p><span style="font-weight: 400;">You’ll also learn words and phrases such as stairs, go out, milk, more, music, runny nose, touch, and mix, medicine, gentle, give, go, grandpa, granddad or grandfather, hurt, juice, jump, kiss, laugh, library, brush teeth, grandma or grandmother, blocks, bubbles, bye, I love you, inside, look, love, dress (get dressed), car, and thank you.</span></p>
<p><span style="font-weight: 400;">More words and phrases include happy, hear, hug, listen, tissue, take turns, swing, sweep, stroller, stick, shoes, sick, sing, slow, and smile, snack, sorry, spill, spit, toilet, potty, poop, play, rice, coat, rattle, read, tree, you&#8217;re welcome, up, pray, spit up, ball, bath, toy, wait, wash hands, wet, heart, sleep, share, and hot.</span></p>
<h3><span style="font-weight: 400;">How You’ll Learn</span></h3>
<p><span style="font-weight: 400;">The course is broken down into 104 videos. Each video involves about 1 minute of work. Concepts are taught through video lectures only.</span></p>

<ul>
<li style="font-weight: 400;" aria-level="1"><a href="https://www.linkedin.com/in/adelaidelawren/" target="_blank" rel="noopener"><span style="font-weight: 400;">Olguin</span></a><span style="font-weight: 400;"> founded TalkBox.Mom to help families start talking in a foreign language (and ASL) the same day they start and reach their goals of becoming at least conversational.</span></li>
